## 🍌 简介

> 🎉 **全网最大的 Nano Banana 提示词库！** 汇聚 **900+ 位全球创作者** 的 **3200+ 精选案例**，持续更新中...

欢迎来到 **AI Art Prompts 精选集**！这是目前最全面的 Gemini Nano Banana / Nano Banana Pro 提示词与生成案例合集。

我们从 X (Twitter)、小红书等全球社交媒体平台精心收集了 **3000+ 高质量提示词**，涵盖摄影、插画、3D 渲染、UI 设计、创意海报等 **20+ 个专业领域**，全方位展示 Google 图像生成模型的无限可能。每个案例都经过人工筛选，确保质量和实用性。

💡 **为什么选择这个项目？**

- 🏆 **规模最大** - 3200+ 提示词，900+ 位创作者，持续增长
- ✅ **质量保证** - 所有案例都是真实生成结果，附带原图展示
- 🎯 **即用即学** - 每个提示词都可直接复制使用，快速上手
- � **每日更新** - 自动化收集最新优质案例，保持时效性
- � **双语支持** - 中英文双语界面，服务全球用户
- 🔗 **完整溯源** - 每个案例都附带原始来源，尊重创作者

> ⭐ **如果这个项目对你有帮助，请点击右上角 Star 支持我们！你的 Star 是我们持续更新的动力！**

添付画像のキャラクターをちびキャラにして。LINEスタンプを作成。表情・ポーズ別・セリフ入で12種類。 https://t.co/BPYBLy5RIB

## 两斤

### [盗梦空间](https://aiart.pics/prompt/inception)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2004806463295009206)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/inception-1.jpg" width="500" alt="盗梦空间">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/inception-2.jpg" width="500" alt="盗梦空间">

```
盗梦空间
Banana Prompt👇
---
​{current_weather} in a gravity-defying {city_name}. The asphalt street curves seamlessly upwards, physically bending 90 degrees to become a vertical wall, then arching directly overhead. Not a reflection, but a solid continuous loop of architecture. Iconic buildings and roads protrude perpendicularly from the curved surface all around. {city_name}'s landmarks hang upside down above. Realistic lighting matching the weather, vivid details, photorealistic 8k. --ar 9:16
```

### [纸雕立体拼贴](https://aiart.pics/prompt/3d-paper-cutout-collage)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2004087291103662152)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251226/3d-paper-cutout-collage-1.jpg" width="500" alt="纸雕立体拼贴">

```
纸雕何必是平面的呢
---
A four-panel photo split collage arranged in a 2x2 grid, presenting four fully layered 3D paper cut-out dioramas.
GLOBAL STYLE (crucial constraint): Every single element in the scene, from the background hills to the central characters and objects, must be constructed from multiple stacked layers of cut matte cardstock. The edges of these paper layers must be visible on all objects, defining their form and volume through layering, not solid sculpting. Soft, warm directional studio lighting casts realistic drop shadows, revealing the thickness and depth of the stacked paper layers everywhere.
Top Left Panel: A forest scene where oversized mushrooms and tiny foxes are built from stacked paper layers.
Top Right Panel: A terraced village where houses and hills are formed by stepped layers of paper.
Bottom Left Panel: Two small figures and a boat made of layered paper, floating on water made of concentric paper layers with layered lanterns.
Bottom Right Panel: A character and a large castle, both constructed from stacked paper layers, on a layered paper cliff.
COLOR PALETTE: Warm, cozy tones of moss green, amber yellow, terracotta orange, deep teal, and creamy white. Octane render, 8k, palpable layered texture. --ar 1:1 --stylize 300
```

### [城市微切片](https://aiart.pics/prompt/city-micro-slice)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2003361642005037179)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251223/city-micro-slice-1.jpg" width="500" alt="城市微切片">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251223/city-micro-slice-2.jpg" width="500" alt="城市微切片">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251223/city-micro-slice-3.jpg" width="500" alt="城市微切片">

```
感谢 @aestheticsguyy 的灵感。
透过世界的某个街角，将一座城市的温度凝缩进这个精致的微观切片之中。
用户只需填入{city_name}即可
Banana Prompt👇
---
A hyper-realistic vertical tilt-shift photograph of a cross-section of a typical building in {city_name} during {current_time}. The current weather is {current_weather}. The scene looks like an intricate miniature diorama. The lighting and sky color accurately reflect the {current_time}, while the street textures and atmosphere visually demonstrate the {current_weather} conditions. At street level, the environment is lifelike. Tiny detailed figures are visible going about their activities. Strong miniature effect with heavy blur at the top and bottom. 8k resolution, volumetric lighting. --ar 9:16
```

### [无缝四分屏纸张合成图像](https://aiart.pics/prompt/seamless-four-quadrant-paper-composite-image)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2002320422046724291)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/seamless-four-quadrant-paper-composite-image-1.jpg" width="500" alt="无缝四分屏纸张合成图像">

```
调了一下午，都快给我调崩溃了
---
A seamless 16:9 full-frame composite image divided into four distinct quadrants. **CRITICAL:** The four sections touch each other directly. NO GREY BACKGROUND. NO BORDERS. NO GAPS. The image is filled edge-to-edge with paper details.
**Composition:** A split-screen view looking deep into four different paper worlds.
1) **Top-Left (Luckin):** A wide view of a magical paper forest. Blue and white paper clouds and coffee leaves fill the quadrant completely. A white paper stag leaps through the density.
2) **Top-Right (Google):** A wide view of a **"Topographic Map" style paper cavern**. The "G" logo is formed by **hundreds of thin sheets** of Blue, Red, Yellow, and Green paper stacked horizontally. It looks like a sediment canyon or a contour map. Visible paper fibers and sharp cut edges. NO plastic smoothness.
3) **Bottom-Left (Coke):** A wide view of a red paper explosion. The Coke bottle is a **Negative Space Silhouette**—a deep hole void cut through dense layers of red paper. White paper ribbons span across the void.
4) **Bottom-Right (McDonald's):** A wide view of a yellow paper city. Vertical strips of yellow paper (french fries) stand densely packing the frame. The Golden Arches rise from deep within the layers.
**Global Material:** Everything is matte cardstock.
**Lighting:** Soft, even studio lighting revealing the depth of the paper cuts.
**Tech:** Octane render, 8k, --ar 16:9 --stylize 400 --no borders, frames, background wall, isolated objects, 3d plastic, seamless texture
```

### [极简雾感石版画](https://aiart.pics/prompt/foggy-minimalist-lithograph)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2001915942243328344)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/foggy-minimalist-lithograph-1.jpg" width="500" alt="极简雾感石版画">

```
感谢原作者 @tisch_eins  的灵感，我好像更喜欢这种风格！
极简构图 + 细腻胶片感 + 一丝中国水墨画的意境
Gemini说这是“Foggy Minimalist Lithograph” (雾感极简石版画风)
Banana Prompt👇
---
A four-panel grid featuring minimalist atmospheric art. The style is faded monochrome photography on high-quality matte paper.Texture & Tone:
Subtle film grain (not heavy noise).
Soft, creamy beige and desaturated grey tones (clean, not dirty).
Low contrast, dreamy, hazy atmosphere.The 4 Panels:
(Top Left): Layered misty mountains with a tiny, sharp silhouette of a modern city at the very bottom.
(Top Right): A lone traveler walking on a smooth sand dune into the fog. Clean lines, vast negative space.
(Bottom Left): The Shanghai skyline (Lujiazui) rising faintly from heavy river mist, ethereal and ghost-like.
(Bottom Right): Abstract zen geometry: concentric water ripples under a large pale sun, with a lone distant skyscraper.Negative Prompt:torn paper, dirt, stains, grunge, scratches, high contrast, harsh lines, blurry, messy, distorted.--ar 1:1 --v 6.0 --style raw
```

### [大胆鲜艳的撞色城市纸雕立体模型](https://aiart.pics/prompt/bold-and-bright-colorful-city-paper-cutout-diorama)

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2001517529932730818)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/bold-and-bright-colorful-city-paper-cutout-diorama-1.jpg" width="500" alt="大胆鲜艳的撞色城市纸雕立体模型">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/bold-and-bright-colorful-city-paper-cutout-diorama-2.jpg" width="500" alt="大胆鲜艳的撞色城市纸雕立体模型">

```
还是喜欢这种大胆鲜艳的撞色
---
1/
Eye-level straight-on view, a hyper-vibrant 3D layered paper cut-out diorama of SHANGHAI city.
The scene showcases iconic Shanghai landmarks: **The Bund waterfront with historic buildings**, **traditional Shikumen alleyways**, and **futuristic Lujiazui skyscrapers (Oriental Pearl Tower, Shanghai Tower)**.
Color Palette: **High contrast palette of Vivid Shanghai Red, Jade Green, and Matte Gold.**
Style & Texture: Playful stylized shapes with smooth curves and clean edges. Material texture is matte cardstock (no gloss).
Physics of Depth: Soft, even studio lighting creates **distinct, realistic deep drop shadows between each individual paper layer**, revealing tangible depth and physical thickness of the matte paper.
Composition: Maximalist, full bleed composition, bursting with intricate details of street life, tiny paper people, and traditional lanterns.
Details: Octane render, 8k, clean details, surreal realism. --ar 3:4 --stylize 450 --no frame, border, box, blurry, digital illustration
2/
Eye-level straight-on view, a hyper-vibrant 3D layered paper cut-out diorama of GUANGZHOU city (The Flower City).
The scene fuses traditional Lingnan culture with modern vitality:
* **Background Layer:** The iconic **Canton Tower (slim waist)** and Zhujiang New Town skyline standing tall.
* **Mid-Ground:** Bustling **Qilou arcade streets** with stained glass windows, filled with crowds enjoying **Yum Cha (Dim Sum)**, stacked steamer baskets, and tea pots.
* **Foreground:** Branches of blooming **Red Kapok flowers** and a festive **Southern Lion (Waking Lion)** head framing the view.
Color Palette: **High contrast palette of Vivid Kapok Red, Emerald Green (Banyan tree tone), and Neon Gold.**
Style & Physics:
* **Material:** Matte cardstock textures.
* **Depth:** Soft studio lighting creates **deep, distinct drop shadows** between the Qilou layers and the tower background, showing the physical spacing of the paper.
* **Vibe:** Maximalist, lively, full of fireworks and life (Yan Huo Qi).
Details: Octane render, 8k, clean edges, surreal realism. --ar 3:4 --stylize 450 --no frame, border, blurry, flat illustration
```

Banana Prompt
---
1/
Eye-level straight-on view, looking directly into a hyper-vibrant 3D layered paper cut-out diorama. glowing China Red and Teal and Gold, extremely high saturation, maximalist composition, crowded festival scene with dragon dance and pagodas. Soft even studio lighting creating deep drop shadows between physical paper layers to define depth, matte paper texture, NO sun rays, NO volumetric lighting, octane render, 8k, clean details --ar 3:4 --stylize 450

Soft even studio lighting creates distinct, realistic drop shadows cast by each individual paper layer onto the layer beneath it, revealing tangible depth and physical thickness of the matte paper. ### [城市/地点名称超写实等距建筑模型](https://aiart.pics/prompt/hyper-realistic-isometric-architectural-maquette-[city-location-name])

**作者**: [@两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2000399808469794843)

```json
{
"prompt": "Subject: [INSERT CITY/LOCATION NAME]. \n\nCreate a hyper-realistic isometric architectural maquette of the Subject, strictly isolated on a seamless pure white studio background. \n\n[Surface Level]: Analyze the Subject to recreate its signature architectural style, vegetation, and street atmosphere. \n- **Architecture**: Representative buildings with authentic materials (e.g., brick, glass, wood) and local design details.\n- **Street Scene**: Localized vehicles, street furniture, and scattered life details appropriate to the location.\n\n[Underground Level]: A deep vertical cross-section revealing underground elements strictly based on the Subject\'s real-world infrastructure:\n- IF it is a modern metropolis: Show complex subway tunnels, maintenance pipes, and concrete foundations.\n- IF it is a historical or rural site: Show rich soil stratification, ancient ruins, sewers, or deep root systems.\n\n[Crucial Lighting & Material Details]: \n1. **Lighting Physics**: The strong sunlight from above must cast distinct, hard shadows from the street level down onto the underground cutaway sections. The underground should be slightly darker, lit by its own dim interior lights (if infrastructure exists) or fading into shadow, creating a contrast with the bright surface.\n2. **Soil Texture**: The earth layers must look realistic and gritty—soil mixed with rocks, gravel, and roots. No smooth textures.\n3. **Photography**: Macro lens photography. Shallow depth of field (tilt-shift focus on the main building) is mandatory. The background MUST be empty white void. \n\n[Technical]: 8k resolution, Unreal Engine 5 render, highly detailed physical model aesthetic.",

"aspect_ratio": "2:3"

prompt

"prompt": "A dramatic, ultra-macro photograph of a genuine [INSERT CURRENCY NAME ONLY], perfectly replicating a high-end miniature art aesthetic. \n\n[Composition]: \n- The banknote is placed **diagonally**, dominating the frame with tight cropping. \n\n[Intelligent Paper Engineering]: \n- **Auto-Subject**: The **signature landscape, architectural motif, or iconic animal** traditionally featured on the reverse side of this specific banknote is identified and rendered as **intricate, multi-layered paper silhouette cutouts** standing vertically from the flat surface. \n- **Style**: The cutout follows the exact contours of the original bill\'s design. The texture is razor-thin, matte currency paper, strictly matching the **authentic color palette** of the specified bill.\n\n[Contextual Miniature]: \n- A hyper-realistic, microscopic **tiny figure or vehicle** that is **culturally and thematically appropriate** to the scenery (e.g., a boat for water, a hiker for mountains, a car for buildings) sits on the flat printed area, interacting with the paper sculpture.\n- A huge, realistic **human thumb** (showing the **fingernail/nail plate**, NOT the fingerprint) dominates the foreground corner to establish scale.\n\n[Photography - The \'Soul\']: \n- **Ultra-shallow depth of field is mandatory**. \n- **Focus Strategy**: Razor-sharp focus ONLY on the tiny miniature model and the ridges of the standing paper cutout. \n- **Bokeh**: The background, foreground text, and finger melt into a **soft, creamy bokeh** that matches the bill\'s dominant color. \n- **Lighting**: Cinematic side-lighting highlighting the intaglio ink and paper fibers.",

}

Inspired by the delicate art of egg carving, intricately depict a grandmother sitting in a rocking chair knitting by a window through elaborate hollow cutouts on a single, complete duck egg shell.
All carved elements are organically connected by thin, delicate shell bridges and lattice structures to maintain structural integrity, ensuring no isolated or floating segments.
The shell surface has a smooth, matte white texture. Gentle, warm backlighting illuminates the shell from within, creating a translucent glow around the cutouts and cozy silhouettes.
Background features a softly blurred rustic living room with a fireplace, providing a nostalgic and warm atmosphere, captured in ultra-detailed 8K resolution for macro-level realism, showing every tiny chisel mark.

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251228/high-end-fashion-magazine-cover-2.jpg" width="500" alt="高端时尚杂志封面">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251228/high-end-fashion-magazine-cover-3.jpg" width="500" alt="高端时尚杂志封面">

```
新做了一个高端时尚杂志封面📷，这次结合了「选区编辑」互动的视觉概念，体现具有冲击力的现代设计感，人物可以自定义。
分享提示词：
一张高端时尚杂志封面。{年轻女性时尚模特}，气质自信前卫，身体张力强，动态姿态，直视镜头。镜头为略低机位仰拍。模特双手比起取景框手势，仿佛与一个矩形选中框有互动，选中框覆盖脸部和肩部。视觉规则：只有选中框内部清晰且为自然彩色；选中框外完全灰度强像素化，无任何颜色或清晰区域。柔和漫射棚拍光。现代编辑感穿搭。版式文字：顶部居中粗体大写扁宽型无衬线标题“FOCUS”，上方小字“DECEMBER 2025”；标题左下“VOL + 随机两位数”；左下角文字块（简短时尚自信标题、短段落、条形码）；右侧“FASHION INTERVIEW”；右下角衬线体小号“THE EDIT”及大号“01-09的随机数字”。模特对标题有遮挡叠加，前后景关系，层次分明，干净现代。字体均为白色，蒙太奇风格字体，文字与图像形成强烈对比。
```

### [时尚质感短片工作流](https://aiart.pics/prompt/fashion-and-texture-short-film-workflow)

**作者**: [@Latte](https://x.com/0xbisc)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0xbisc/status/1999344734595350744)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251222/fashion-and-texture-short-film-workflow-cover-1.jpg" width="500" alt="时尚质感短片工作流">

```
这个工作流可以稳定输出时尚质感短片
受到 @ReflctWillie 和 @underwoodxie96 的启发，突然有了灵感，也想试试看。整个流程比想象中更可控，而且每一步都有明确的作用。
这个视频的生成教程：
1. 生成一张基础人物图
2. 将图像导入 Nano Banana Pro，使用提示词：在一个 3×3 的网格中展示这个角色，从不同的角度呈现，单色的渐变背景，姿势随机。
如果需要特定姿势，直接在提示词中指定即可。
3. 生成后截图喜欢的关键帧，然后使用提示词：放大到 4K。得到高清图片
4. 使用 Kling 2.5 Turbo 将首尾帧变成视频，提示词：摄影机在摇臂上缓慢平稳地下降
5. 使用 @ReflctWillie 开发的速度曲线工具使用预设调整每个片段的播放节奏，最后拼接成完整视频。
对比在传统剪辑软件慢慢调试实在方便太多。
自从有了 AI 之后，每个人都可以高效地开发出解决痛点的小工具，让我们可以把更多精力投入到创意本身，而不是被技术细节困住，这个转变真的很棒。
```

    "场景": "陌生外星星球地表，作为临时停泊与检修地点",
    "地貌": "外星地表以简洁的岩石、沙砾或柔和起伏的地形为主，形态抽象克制，避免杂乱细节",
    "氛围": "空气清澈，少量漂浮尘埃增强尺度感，整体氛围安静、从容，具有高级电影感",
    "背景": "远处简洁的外星建筑轮廓与地平线，建筑后方竖立着标志性的金色拱门标志，像霓虹灯一样柔和闪耀；天空中可见一到数颗遥远的行星，体量克制、边缘柔和，作为背景存在，增强宇宙纵深与科幻感"
  },
  "美学风格": {
    "光影": "温暖定向光集中表现汉堡的食物质感，金色拱门霓虹光作为背景氛围光，与冷色外星环境光形成柔和对比，光影层次清晰，画面不显拥挤",
    "风格": "电影级广告视觉，画面简洁、现代、克制，超现实但高度真实，强烈食欲感与轻度科幻探索感并存，具有记忆点"
  },
  "元信息": {
    "画幅比例": "9:16",
    "参考指令": "画面构图与整体风格需与上传的参考图保持一致"
  }
}
```

## 0x卡卡撸特 | Golden.S

### [《诡秘之主》海报设计](https://aiart.pics/prompt/the-master-of-mysteries-poster-design)

**作者**: [@0x卡卡撸特 | Golden.S](https://x.com/0xkakarot888)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/0xkakarot888/status/1998381269118533823)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251215/the-master-of-mysteries-poster-design-1.jpg" width="500" alt="《诡秘之主》海报设计">

```
太顶了，最近在二刷《诡秘之主》，用nano banana pro做了一张海报，这美学太震撼了！
提示词：
请为影视剧/小说《需要添加的名称》设计一张高品质的3D海报，需要先检索影视剧/小说信息和著名的片段场景。  首先，请利用你的知识库检索这个影视剧/小说的内容，找出一个最具代表性的名场面或核心地点。在画面中央，将这个场景构建为一个精致的轴侧视角3D微缩模型。
风格要采用梦工厂动画那种细腻、柔和的渲染风格。你需要还原当时的建筑细节、人物动态以及环境氛围，无论是暴风雨还是宁静的午后，都要自然地融合在模型的光影里。  关于背景，不要使用简单的纯白底。请在模型周围营造一种带有淡淡水墨晕染和流动光雾的虚空环境，色调雅致，让画面看起来有呼吸感和纵深感，衬托出中央模型的珍贵。
最后是底部的排版，请生成中文文字。居中写上小说名称，字体要有与原著风格匹配的设计感。在书名下方，自动检索并排版一句原著中关于该场景的经典描写或台词，字体使用优雅的衬线体。整体布局要像一个高级的博物馆藏品铭牌那样精致平衡。
```

画像生成はどうせすぐ飽和する。
参入障壁が低いから、誰でも出来るし、競争もすぐ激化する。
っていう未来はたぶん正しい。
でも逆に言えば、誰でも出来る今ってめちゃくちゃチャンスでもある。
「画像生成で稼ごう」とか「マネタイズしよう」とか、いきなり考えなくて良い。
ガチの初心者なら、まずは何も考えず遊んでみるのが一番。
日本語でもそれっぽいの出るし、英語でも中国語でもプロンプト次第でどんどん面白くなる。
いちいち正解探さなくて良い。ただ触ってみる。それだけで十分。
無料で使えて、生成制限もないGoogleのImageFXとかから始めるのがオススメ。
ツールもプロンプトも、まずは触ることから全部始まる。
ちな、このポストの画像で使ったプロンプトはリプ欄に貼っとく👇

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/23rd_Pulikesi/status/2001549121908617489)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/cinematic-studio-portrait-photography-1.jpg" width="500" alt="现代电影式肖像摄影">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/cinematic-studio-portrait-photography-2.jpg" width="500" alt="现代电影式肖像摄影">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/cinematic-studio-portrait-photography-3.jpg" width="500" alt="现代电影式肖像摄影">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251219/cinematic-studio-portrait-photography-4.jpg" width="500" alt="现代电影式肖像摄影">

```
1. Open ChatGPT
2. Upload your picture
3.Enter the prompt —
"A cinematic studio portrait of the person in the uploaded photo, framed from the chest up, facing the camera with a calm, confident presence.
Dramatic dual-tone lighting with cool teal and warm golden tones creating a modern, cinematic mood.
Natural skin texture, sharp focus on the eyes, soft shadows, and smooth color transitions.
Hair styled naturally, wearing a minimal dark outfit with a contemporary aesthetic.
Clean studio background with subtle gradients.
Professional photography, shallow depth of field, cinematic color grading, ultra-realistic, high detail, 4K quality.
Aspect ratio: 3:4 "
```

### [无茶振り海报选手权](https://aiart.pics/prompt/wuta-zhenri-poster-contest)

**作者**: [@角煮星丸](https://x.com/_3912657840)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/_3912657840/status/1999617202153292065)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251214/wuta-zhenri-poster-contest-1.jpg" width="500" alt="无茶振り海报选手权">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251214/wuta-zhenri-poster-contest-2.jpg" width="500" alt="无茶振り海报选手权">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251214/wuta-zhenri-poster-contest-3.jpg" width="500" alt="无茶振り海报选手权">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251214/wuta-zhenri-poster-contest-4.jpg" width="500" alt="无茶振り海报选手权">

```
✨ 無茶振りポスター選手権✨
prompt
--------
このキャラクターでめっちゃかっこいいポスターを作って。
ポーズとか構図も自由に考えていいからとにかくめっちゃカッコよくして。
Silent Belly, Holy Nightっていうテキストをカッコよく入れて。
--------
上記の舐めてる丸投げ日本語プロンプトで、各社モデルにキャラの正面立ち絵のキャラ参照画像を渡して、カッコいいポスター画像を3枚ずつ生成してもらいます。見せられないレベルの破綻した画像は作り直して減点です。
一番バリエーション豊かでカッコよかったモデルが優勝です。
採点基準は私の気分です。
画像から参加した4モデルがわかったら凄い。
⚠️ガチの性能比較じゃなくてお遊び企画ですから参考にしないで下さい。
ちゃんとした生成結果が欲しいならプロンプトは真面目に書きましょう。
```

## こーたろー/営業×AIの人生再設計士

### [マーケティングの5ステップ円環状図解](https://aiart.pics/prompt/marketing-5-step-circular-diagram)

**作者**: [@こーたろー/営業×AIの人生再設計士](https://x.com/56major)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/56major/status/1997459106157002773)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/marketing-5-step-circular-diagram-1.jpg" width="500" alt="マーケティングの5ステップ円環状図解">

```
Nano Banana Proって
使いこなせれば最強なんだけど
指示のクオリティーに左右されます！
この画像も以下のプロンプトで
作成できますのでご参考に↓
〜プロンプト〜
「マーケティングの流れ」を、5ステップの円環状（サークル図）で 時計回りに表現した図解を作成してください。
【全体スタイル】
・白背景のシンプルでビジネス向けの図解
・円形のフローチャートを時計回りに5分割
・ブルー系のアクセントカラーで統一
・日本語テキストを正確・見やすく描画
・スライド資料にそのまま貼れる整ったデザイン
【円環の5ステップ（時計回り）】
円の外周に以下5項目を配置し、太めの矢印でつないでください。
1. 市場理解      - 市場・競合・顧客を調査
2. ターゲット設定      - 狙う顧客層を決める
3. 価値提案（バリュープロポジション）      - 選ばれる理由をつくる
4. 施策設計（4P＋集客導線）      - 商品・価格・売り方・伝え方を組み立てる
5. 分析と改善（PDCA）
- データを見て改善し次のアクションへ
【レイアウト条件】
・円の外側に角丸ボックスで「タイトル＋短い説明」を配置
・各ステップには線画アイコンを1つ付ける
・中心に「マーケティングの5ステップ」と記載
・矢印は時計回りの流れが明確にわかるように配置
・余白多めで洗練された構図 【禁止事項】 ・人物写真は使用しない
・実在企業名やロゴを入れない
【完成イメージ】
マーケティングの基本プロセスが5つの要素で ひと目で理解できる円環状のビジネス図解。 スライドや提案資料にそのまま使える品質。
#NanoBananaPro #プロンプト
```

### [梦幻IMAX 70mm电影肖像](https://aiart.pics/prompt/dreamy-imax-70mm-film-portrait)

**作者**: [@Nehuen](https://x.com/8AIEnthusiast9)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/8AIEnthusiast9/status/1998046026649768190)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/dreamy-imax-70mm-film-portrait-1.jpg" width="500" alt="梦幻IMAX 70mm电影肖像">

```
Amazing results based on a prompt by @rjchicago with some changes for Nano Banana Pro!
PROMPT: A dreamy IMAX 70mm film portrait, mid-shot, of a young woman with a gentle, distant expression.
Her hair is in a loose, chic updo with soft tendrils framing her face, wearing a fitted ribbed black wool turtleneck.
The scene is dramatically lit by opposing magenta and teal colored gels, creating volumetric haze and soft bloom halation around highlights on her skin and hair.
The background is a wash of pastel city light bokeh from a Parisian window at night.
Film grain present, extremely shallow depth of field (f/1.2), natural skin textures, ethereal and elegant mood, cinematic color grade.
```

## 就是玩AI

### [街头霸王游戏人物志艺术升华版](https://aiart.pics/prompt/artistic-elevation-street-fighter-character-portfolio)

**作者**: [@就是玩AI](https://x.com/94vanAI)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/94vanAI/status/2006259527679893546)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251231/artistic-elevation-street-fighter-character-portfolio-1.jpg" width="500" alt="街头霸王游戏人物志艺术升华版">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251231/artistic-elevation-street-fighter-character-portfolio-2.jpg" width="500" alt="街头霸王游戏人物志艺术升华版">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251231/artistic-elevation-street-fighter-character-portfolio-3.jpg" width="500" alt="街头霸王游戏人物志艺术升华版">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251231/artistic-elevation-street-fighter-character-portfolio-4.jpg" width="500" alt="街头霸王游戏人物志艺术升华版">

```
刷到@servasyy_ai黄总的这个街头霸王游戏人物志的提示词，我突然想到了一个万能用法，不单单是游戏了，很多方面都可以做艺术升华。改了一个通用版本（带有立体感）提示词:指南手册通用版提示词：看起来有那种商业渲染味道了，放进PPT里面观感绝佳！！喜欢的可以尝试各种元素，都可以通用！！！
[BRAND NAME]: [品牌名称，例如 Nintendo / Riot Games / FromSoftware / Klei Entertainment 等]
A high-end, glossy concept art magazine editorial photograph of a unique, unexpected functional object conceptualized and designed by [品牌名称]: a premium collector's edition [手册/图鉴/攻略书/生存手札/帝国典籍/远征编年史 等自定义名称] for [游戏完整名称，例如 The Legend of Zelda: Tears of the Kingdom / League of Legends / Elden Ring] on [平台，例如 Nintendo Switch 2 / PC / PlayStation 5], crafted as an ultra-luxurious, sculptural artifact that captures the [游戏核心氛围关键词，例如 epic mystical grandeur / vibrant strategic depth / dark gothic whimsy / high-octane adrenaline] with refined minimalist elegance – a thick hardcover tome opened to reveal intricately illustrated pages of [列出主要内页内容，例如 world maps, boss strategies, ability trees, character profiles, crafting recipes, lore timelines 等].
**1. The Concept & Object (AI Invention):**
The [手册名称] reimagines the [游戏] guide as a [形容词 + 物件类型，例如 sacred relic / forbidden grimoire / imperial war manual / high-stakes tactical codex]: substantial yet [氛围形容词，例如 enigmatic / commanding / adventurous / ominous] (approx. [尺寸，例如 240x300mm] when open), with a [闭合方式，例如 magnetic clasp / heavy magnetic closure flap] featuring an embossed glowing [标志性元素，例如 Erdtree / Hextech crystal / Master Sword / Horizon Festival logo] on the cover, [丝带颜色] silk ribbon bookmark, reinforced [材质] corners, and die-cut windows revealing layered [纸张风格，例如 vellum / parchment / silk-scroll] pages. Interior spreads showcase hyper-detailed [主要内容，例如 raid layouts / Summoner's Rift topography / Constant biomes / Mexico map biomes] with [具体功能，例如 wipe mech timelines / optimal ward spots / jungle clear paths / boss phase breakdowns], [其他内容] charts, and narrative timelines [连接游戏元素，例如 of the Golden Order / of Runeterra regions / from the Shattering]. It feels like a [比喻，例如 relic unearthed from the Erdtree’s roots / forbidden archive from the Institute of War] while serving as the ultimate functional companion for [玩家身份，例如 Tarnished / summoners / survivors / raiders].
**2. Materials & Details (Hyper-Premium):**
Constructed from ultra-premium, highly tactile materials inspired by [游戏美学关键词，例如 Tears of the Kingdom’s epic fantasy / League’s futuristic-fantasy / Don\'t Starve’s gothic whimsy]: hand-bound cover in [主色调，例如 deep midnight-blue / imperial-red / charcoal-black] Italian calfskin or premium Alcantara with subtle [质感，例如 pearlescent shift / cracked patina / silk brocade weave] and [箔色] foil-embossed title "[手册标题，例如 TEARS OF THE KINGDOM COMPANION ARCHIVE]", interior pages on thick [克重，例如 160gsm] textured [纸张类型，例如 cotton paper / vellum / rice paper] mimicking [风格，例如 ancient stone tablets / silk scrolls / aged explorer notes] with faint [水印元素，例如 glowing rune / ink brush / shadow] watermarks, spot UV gloss highlighting [高光元素，例如 Zonai devices / ability icons / nightmare fuel / car liveries], precision metallic foil accents ([颜色] for [元素，例如 rose gold for constructs / chrome silver for hextech]), hand-stitched binding with visible [对比色] contrast thread, and tactile embossing for [纹理，例如 sky island topography / web patterns / tentacle spikes / road textures]. Hyper-realistic details: visible leather grain and [氛围] patina, microscopic paper fiber [质感，例如 antiquity / vibrancy], delicate page curls with [阴影风格] shadows, holographic foil [标志性符号，例如 Elden Ring sigils / League emblems], chamfered [边缘材质] edges, and complex layered contrasts between matte [纸张], glossy illustrations, and shimmering [箔色] embellishments.
**3. Photography & Lighting (Cinematic Studio):**
Shot on a medium format Phase One camera with a 100mm macro lens. Extremely shallow depth of field, razor-sharp focus on hero details (open spread with [主要焦点，例如 sky island map / Summoner's Rift map / Constant biome map], [箔色] foil [元素], embossed [标志], stitching, glowing [效果]) and creamy, smooth bokeh background. Sophisticated studio softbox lighting: gentle enveloping fill light with precise rim lighting to accentuate leather contours, paper tactility, metallic reflections, and subtle [氛围] glows on illustrated elements.
**4. Environment:**
Seamless, impeccably clean studio cyclorama background in a pure ultra-light pastel tone ([氛围色调，例如 epic pale sky azure / intense hextech blue / moody lunar gray / vibrant sunset orange]), completely free of shadows.
**5. Layout & UI Elements (Strict Placement):**
- **Bottom Right Corner:** Small, understated, monochrome gray [品牌logo，例如 Nintendo / Riot Games / Klei Entertainment] logo paired with subtle [标志性图标，例如 glowing Zonai dragon / League pentagon / shadow hand].
- **Bottom Left Corner:** Small, minimalist monochrome gray text describing the product. Font: Manrope Regular with very tight tracking (kerning) and balanced line spacing. Format:
"CONCEPT STUDY: [手册名称].
MATERIAL: [主要材质组合，例如 ITALIAN CALFSKIN, GOLD FOIL, TEXTURED VELLUM PARCHMENT].
SS25."

超级大类别1: 写实高级肖像类（Photorealistic & Artistic Portraits）
这些提示词支持单人/多人，多种照片质感（超写实、电影、复古、梦幻），强调真实皮肤纹理、光影反射、节日细节（如烟花、香槟、倒计时）。可上传真人照片作为参考，实现高度个性化还原。｛Prompt：

超级大类别2: 卡通插图类（Cartoon & Illustration Styles）
这些提示词覆盖所有主流画风（动漫、迪士尼、皮克斯、Chibi/Kawaii、复古卡通、混合），支持单人/多人，强调可爱夸张表情、活力节日元素。可上传真人照片作为参考，转为卡通版本（保留可辨识面部特征）。
｛Prompt：
based on the uploaded reference photo (if any), transform into [anime / Disney / Pixar 3D / chibi kawaii / vintage cartoon / mixed art style] illustration of [a cute character / multiple adorable friends / a group of whimsical figures] celebrating New Year 2026, [solo big expressive eyes / group cheering with party hats] [holding sparklers / toasting / blowing horns], vibrant festive background with confetti explosion, balloons, 2026 banner and magical fireworks, [detailed digital art / soft pastel colors / exaggerated joyful expressions / polished animation style], high energy cute and fun atmosphere, masterpiece｝

```
Subject：Cinematic hyper-realistic movie stills in comic page format, full comic page with 5 panels and thick black panel gutters, ultra-detailed photorealistic rendering, shot on 70mm IMAX film with professional cinema camera, glossy neon candy palette (electric cyan, magenta, violet, acid lime), extreme glitch-sparkle particles and star confetti explosively drifting across every panel, heavy halftone + screenprint texture overlay, ultra high contrast cinematic lighting with luminous volumetric gradients and god rays. She looks curious and deeply awed. Panel plan (strict layout): Top-left: extreme close-up portrait, hair dramatically sweeping in wind, galaxy glitter and lens flares behind her face. Top-right: wide full-body cinematic shot in the crystal forest, dramatic soft rim lighting and volumetric glow around her hands. Middle-left: dramatic foreshortened hand reaching directly toward camera, massive prismatic energy streaming like intense rainbow aurora ribbons with heavy particle effects. Bottom-left: two hands in elegant mid-gesture, overwhelming sparkling cosmic light pouring and overflowing between fingers with intense sparkle and bokeh. Bottom-right: hand unleashing a massive glitchy neon energy burst, explosive light rays, pixel fragments, chromatic aberration, and shockwave effects. Typography (optional): huge onomatopoeia in bold gradient comic lettering with Japanese text, thick white outline and heavy drop shadow: 「星の光！」「幻視！」「粒子嵐！」 Maximum cinematic special effects, intense lens flares, anamorphic bokeh, motion blur, dynamic camera angles, epic scale, ultra-detailed VFX, vibrant, energetic, breathtaking, photorealistic Korean K-pop idol face seamlessly integrated into hyper-stylized surreal environment.

# Prompt:

**作者**: [@荒井健一 AK](https://x.com/aarai666)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/aarai666/status/1998732651851583896)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251210/3d-poster-design-for-romance-of-the-three-kingdoms-classic-scene-1.jpg" width="500" alt="《三国演义》名场面3D海报设计">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251210/3d-poster-design-for-romance-of-the-three-kingdoms-classic-scene-2.jpg" width="500" alt="《三国演义》名场面3D海报设计">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251210/3d-poster-design-for-romance-of-the-three-kingdoms-classic-scene-3.jpg" width="500" alt="《三国演义》名场面3D海报设计">

```
これいいね。
prompt：请为影视剧/小说《三国演义》设计一张高品质的3D海报，需要先检索影视剧/小说信息和著名的片段场景。
首先，请利用你的知识库检索这个影视剧/小说的内容，找出一个最具代表性的名场面或核心地点。在画面中央，将这个场景构建为一个精致的轴侧视角3D微缩模型。风格要采用梦工厂动画那种细腻、柔和的渲染风格。你需要还原当时的建筑细节、人物动态以及环境氛围，无论是暴风雨还是宁静的午后，都要自然地融合在模型的光影里。
关于背景，不要使用简单的纯白底。请在模型周围营造一种带有淡淡水墨晕染和流动光雾的虚空环境，色调雅致，让画面看起来有呼吸感和纵深感，衬托出中央模型的珍贵。
最后是底部的排版，请生成中文文字。居中写上小说名称，字体要有与原著风格匹配的设计感。在书名下方，自动检索并排版一句原著中关于该场景的经典描写或台词，字体使用优雅的衬线体。整体布局要像一个高级的博物馆藏品铭牌那样精致平衡。
```

{
  "retexture_mode": "shape_lock",

    "preserve_silhouette": true,
    "geometry_sensitive_mapping": true,
    "detail_retention": "keep contours, folds, and depth variations"
  },

      "hollow injection-molded shells",
      "snap-fit joints",
      "peg locks",
      "rotating axles"
    ]
  },

    "type": "studio spotlight",
    "direction": "front and overhead",
    "color": "warm white",
    "mood": "fun and playful"
  },
  "background": {
    "type": "gradient backdrop",
    "color": "pastel rainbow fade"
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "front view",
    "focus": "sharp",
    "depth_of_field": "shallow"
  },
  "color_palette": {
    "dominant": [
      "bubblegum pink",
      "sky blue",
      "lemon yellow"
    ],

      "white",

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/_abranko_/thread/1938936595257688552)

```
用Yaseen 的蛋糕系灵感，修改了格蕾塔风·时尚单品悬浮系列，这个也很有高级感！可以拿去打广告了！
Nano Banana prompt 👇
Create a professional 2x2 quad-grid cinematic composition featuring four distinct luxury lifestyle images. Each panel must strictly adhere to the Greta Gerwig visionary aesthetic: bright, warm, and playful yet chic.
Universal Technical Standards for all panels: All images must use an ARRI Alexa 65 camera profile with Kodak Portra 400 film stock emulation for natural skin tones and fine grain. Lighting is a cinematic soft glow with high diffusion against a flat studio bone off-white background. Every item is in a graphic centered symmetry and a zero-gravity suspended animation state.
Panel 1 (Top-Left - High Jewelry): A floating 18K gold diamond necklace and emerald earrings. Include fluid effects of crystalline water ripples and scattered fine gold leaf debris.
Panel 2 (Top-Right - Skincare): A frosted glass skincare bottle with a gold pump. Feature translucent liquid amber swirls, floating fragrance mist, and small chamomile flower debris.
Panel 3 (Bottom-Left - Tech): Transparent wireless earbuds and a retro-futuristic digital camera. Add ethereal pastel sound waves, glistening light beams, and floating minimalist geometric shards.
Panel 4 (Bottom-Right - Fashion): A miniature structured leather handbag and a floral silk scarf. Incorporate soft air currents flowing the scarf, with floating pearl beads and fresh spring blossoms.
Output Requirement: Present as a single high-resolution image divided into a seamless 2x2 grid. Total aspect ratio 9:16.
```

A cinematic medium shot of a stunning woman standing on a busy snowy street at night. She has flawless porcelain pale skin and exquisite, delicate facial features. Nano Banana prompt👇
一只手拿着智能手机，背景是有落叶和绿色长椅的秋季公园。手机屏幕上显示着一张**{主体}的生动照片。手机屏幕内的背景景观与手机后方真实的虚化背景完美对齐，创造出一种透明的错觉。屏幕上画有白色的手写文字注释和箭头，指向{主体}**的特征。柔和的自然光，照片级真实感，4k分辨率，高细节，创意社交媒体摄影风格。3D 弹出效果：上半身从屏幕中浮现，下半身留在用户界面内。{主体}**的图片如图，保留面部和外形特征不做任何改变。

### [圣诞风格心情愉悦的创意拼贴](https://aiart.pics/prompt/cheerful-christmas-themed-creative-collage)

**作者**: [@Adam也叫吉米](https://x.com/Adam38363368936)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/Adam38363368936/status/2003025725675204789)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251223/cheerful-christmas-themed-creative-collage-1.jpg" width="500" alt="圣诞风格心情愉悦的创意拼贴">

```
圣诞风格看着让人心情大好！
结合 @SimplyAnnisa 的灵感，创作了这个prompt，试验了好几遍终于复刻了。
注意要点：
1.人物脸部特征不要发生任何变化（Use the face without any  change）
2.右上和右下图有关键连接，而不是独立的。
Nano Banana Prompt👇
Use the face without any  change.A high-quality 2x2 creative photo collage of a young woman with long wavy black hair , posing inside cardboard boxes for a Christmas-themed challenge. She wears a cream, red, and green Fair Isle knit sweater.
Layout & Interaction (Crucial):The right side features a continuous action across two panels. Red wine is poured from the top-right panel and flows vertically down into the bottom-right panel.
Panel Details:
Top Left: She blows artificial snow from her palms towards the camera.
Bottom Left: She holds glowing fairy lights and a red bauble, smiling warmly.
Top Right: She leans on the box edge, holding a wine bottle, pouring red wine downwards so the liquid stream exits the bottom of this frame.
Bottom Right: She is positioned below, holding a wine glass that catches the stream of wine pouring down from the panel above. She is looking up, watching the wine flow into her glass.
Style: Creative box challenge photography, seamless cross-panel interaction, festive mood, soft studio lighting, ultra-realistic textures.
```

```
一起来探索微缩世界
prompt👇 https://t.co/vW7GvF2iYc
1. 电子复古风——复古游戏机大修
这个场景将一个巨大的旧 Game Boy 变成了繁忙的维修工地。
A wide-angle, tilt-shift macro photograph of a colossal vintage gray Game Boy handheld console being overhauled by a swarm of miniature technicians. The console is surrounded by intricate scaffolding. A miniature crane is lifting a glowing replacement LCD screen component into place. Other tiny workers use enormous cotton swabs to clean the cartridge slot, while a team welders works on exposed circuit boards near the 'A' and 'B' buttons. The plastic shows realistic wear and scratches. The setting is a cluttered electronics workbench. Shallow depth of field, cinematic lighting. --ar 4:3 --v 6.0
2. 梦幻甜品风——云端蛋糕摩天楼
这个场景将一个多层婚礼蛋糕想象成一座正在封顶的摩天大楼。
A wide-angle, tilt-shift macro photograph of a towering, multi-tiered wedding cake under construction, acting as a skyscraper. Miniature bakers behave like construction workers: teams are plastering thick white frosting onto the sides like concrete masonry, tower cranes lift massive sugar-paste flower decorations to the top tier, and workers rappel down the sides on ropes, sprinkling giant silver dragées. Scaffolding wraps around the lower tiers. The setting is an elegant dessert table. Soft, glamorous lighting, rich textures of icing and sugar. --ar 4:3 --v 6.0
3. 自然田园风——巨型向日葵收割
这个场景将一朵向日葵的花盘变成了一个繁忙的农业收割基地。
A wide-angle, tilt-shift macro photograph of a colossal blooming sunflower head serving as a busy agricultural operation site. Miniature farmers drive micro-combine harvesters across the central disc florets, collecting massive golden pollen granules. Teams use miniature fire hoses to water the vibrant yellow petals, while others use tiny chainsaws to trim giant green leaves at the base. Scaffolding is built around the stem. The setting is a sunny garden patch during golden hour. Highly detailed natural textures. --ar 4:3 --v 6.0
4.潮流工业风——潮流球鞋工地
一只巨大的潮流球鞋想象成一座正在进行最后组装的宏伟建筑
A wide-angle, tilt-shift macro photograph of a giant, colorful high-top sneaker acting as a major construction site. Miniature workers are rappelling down the thick shoelaces which resemble heavy bridge cables to tighten them. Teams of painters on scaffolding are applying the final coat of color to the iconic logo on the side, while others at the base are cementing the thick rubber sole. The texture of the leather and canvas is magnified. The setting is inside a giant shoebox. Streetwear aesthetic, vibrant colors, shallow depth of field. --ar 4:3 --v 6.0
```

### [敦煌壁画雷神遗迹之谜](https://aiart.pics/prompt/dunhuang-mural-thunder-god-relics-mystery)

**作者**: [@浮海一樂 Aether](https://x.com/AetherWu)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AetherWu/status/1997975468482740573)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251208/dunhuang-mural-thunder-god-relics-mystery-1.jpg" width="500" alt="敦煌壁画雷神遗迹之谜">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251208/dunhuang-mural-thunder-god-relics-mystery-2.jpg" width="500" alt="敦煌壁画雷神遗迹之谜">

```
1. A magnificent flying portrait of Thor, the Norse God of Thunder, rendered in the ethereal Dunhuang Apsara (Flying celestial) painting style. Thor is depicted in dynamic mid-flight motion, soaring through celestial clouds with supernatural grace and divine power. His muscular heroic physique shows the strength of a warrior deity, yet his pose captures the elegant floating movement characteristic of Dunhuang flying apsaras. He wears a unique fusion of Norse and celestial elements: ornate Viking armor with golden embossed patterns of thunderbolts and ravens, flowing crimson and azure silk ribbons that billow dramatically in divine winds, a magnificent cape that streams behind him like celestial clouds painted in gold and ultramarine, elaborate Norse arm rings and belt decorated with runic inscriptions and hammer motifs. His iconic flaming red beard and long hair flow dynamically as if caught in eternal divine wind. In his powerful right hand he firmly grasps Mjolnir, his legendary hammer,
2. A majestic full-body portrait of Hua Mulan, the legendary Chinese female warrior, rendered in the sacred Dunhuang mural painting style. Mulan stands in a powerful yet graceful pose, dressed in elaborate Tang Dynasty military armor with intricate golden patterns and decorative motifs. Her armor features layered plates with cloud and phoenix designs, flowing red and gold silk sashes, and ornate shoulder guards. She holds a gleaming sword with ceremonial tassels, her posture dignified and heroic. Her face shows delicate feminine features with a determined expression, hair tied in a traditional warrior's topknot adorned with golden ornaments. The background features the characteristic Dunhuang aesthetic: rich ochre and burnt sienna tones, faded ancient textures suggesting weathered cave walls, floating celestial clouds in gold and crimson, decorative floral borders with lotus and peony motifs. Golden halos and divine light rays emanate around her figure, emphasizing her sacred heroic statu
```

### [纳米香蕉专业提示](https://aiart.pics/prompt/nano-banana-professional-prompt)

**作者**: [@AshutoshShrivastava](https://x.com/ai_for_success)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/ai_for_success/status/2001908107392504256)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/nano-banana-professional-prompt-1.jpg" width="500" alt="纳米香蕉专业提示">

```json
Nano-banana pro prompt.
How to use : Upload reference image along with this prompt.
{
"subject_core": {
"demographics": "[STRICTLY FOLLOW REFERENCE IMAGE]: Age, gender, and ethnicity must match the uploaded source photo exactly. Rendered as a hyper-realistic graphite sketch.",
"body_type": "Matches reference image physique, appearing to lean forward out of the 2D plane",
"facial_features": "High-fidelity graphite translation of the reference face; shading emphasizes specific bone structure and unique traits from the source photo; eyes detailed with paper-white catchlights",
"hair": "Matches reference image hairstyle and texture exactly, rendered with varying pencil pressure (hatching and cross-hatching)"
},
"subject_styling": {
"makeup_grooming": "Matches reference image grooming standards; skin texture converted to realistic pencil grain and stippling",
"expression": "Matches reference image expression (e.g., focused, smiling, or neutral), intense gaze directed relative to the viewer",
"pose_action": "Anamorphic illusion: The subject\'s hand (drawn in graphite) creates a 3D effect, appearing to reach out of the flat paper surface, holding a realistic wooden pencil"
},
"wardrobe": {
"top": "Matches clothing from reference image, textures converted to graphite cross-hatching to imply fabric weight",
"bottom": "N/A (cropped or fading into the white of the paper)",
"footwear": "N/A",
"accessories": "Any distinct accessories from the reference photo rendered in sketch format"
},
"environment_context": {
"location": "Macro view of a textured, heavy-tooth white sketchbook page resting on a dark rustic wooden surface",
"background_elements": "Real-world objects resting on the paper to sell the scale: a worn white block eraser, a metal pencil sharpener, scattered cedar wood pencil shavings, smudge of graphite dust",
"time_context": "Studio lighting environment, timeless artistic setting"
},
"cinematography_and_tech": {
"lighting": "Dual lighting setup: 1. Simulated shading within the sketch based on the reference. 2. External \'real world\' harsh lamp light casting long shadows from the pencil and eraser onto the paper",
"camera_gear": "Macro photography, 100mm lens, sharp focus on the paper texture",
"framing": "Top-down flat lay or slight isometric angle to enhance the \'pop-up\' 3D illusion of the sketch",
"visual_fidelity": "Photorealistic rendering of paper grain/fiber, tactile graphite sheen, rough charcoal texture, high contrast between dark leads and white paper",
"color_grading": "Monochromatic greyscale for the subject (graphite/charcoal tones), natural realistic colors for the desk and drawing tools"
},
"aspect_ratio": "4:5"
}
```

**作者**: [@ai.gezgini](https://x.com/ai_gezgini)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/ai_gezgini/status/2004875573806485915)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/parchment-series-memory-of-cities-1.jpg" width="500" alt="Parşömen Serisi | Şehirlerin Hafızası">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/parchment-series-memory-of-cities-3.jpg" width="500" alt="Parşömen Serisi | Şehirlerin Hafızası">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/parchment-series-memory-of-cities-4.jpg" width="500" alt="Parşömen Serisi | Şehirlerin Hafızası">

```
📜 Parşömen Serisi | Şehirlerin Hafızası ⏳
🏛 Antik uygarlıkların temelleri
🕌 İmparatorlukların yükselişi
🌉 Ticaret yolları ve dönüşüm
🏙 Bugünün yaşayan şehirleri
Geçmişten günümüze bir şehrin hafızası,
eski bir parşömen arşivinden taşarak
katman katman, üç boyutlu olarak canlanıyor.
✍️ Favori şehrini yaz.
Prompt:
👇
Hyper-realistic 3D isometric masterpiece, set against a magnificent, endless traditional ink-wash historical parchment scroll unfurling across the background.
The scene visualizes the historical memory, cultural layers, ancient civilizations, architectural evolution, symbolic identity, and present-day essence of ([buraya favori şehrini yaz]), interpreted through iconic architectural landmarks with construction dates, ancient symbols, handwritten historical annotations, and fully three-dimensional city-specific forms  all emerging directly from the parchment as a living, chronological urban archive.
The parchment behaves like a continuous historical timeline, clearly marking construction dates of major structures, era transitions, and transformational milestones, connecting antiquity, medieval periods, early modern eras, and the contemporary city into a single, visually traceable narrative.
At the center of the composition, the city’s present-day symbolic landmarks appear as fully realized, hyper-realistic 3D structures, rising outward from the parchment and representing the city’s current identity, skyline, and daily life.
IMPORTANT TEXT RULE (MANDATORY)
ALL visible text inside the image — including calligraphy, annotations, notes, captions, maps, timelines, labels, arrows, stamps, seals, dates, and written explanations — MUST BE IN TURKISH.
NO English words are visible anywhere inside the image.
Parchment Annotations
(Content-Adaptive – Urban Memory & Architecture Archive)
The parchment contains aged handwritten Turkish calligraphy, historical cartographic sketches, architectural blueprints, city maps, timeline arrows, symbolic seals, and marginal notes that automatically adapt to the city written in parentheses.
For each city, the parchment MUST include the following clearly separated Turkish-written sections:
• Şehrin Kimliği & Coğrafi Konumu
Şehrin adı
Bulunduğu coğrafya
Stratejik ve kültürel önemi
Doğal sınırlar ve ticaret yolları
Sunulumu: El yazısı arşiv notları, kenar açıklamaları, pusula ve harita eskizleri.
• Sembolik Yapılar & İnşa Tarihleri — ZORUNLU
Şehri temsil eden ana yapılar, her biri için açık inşa tarihleriyle birlikte gösterilmelidir.
Her yapı için:
Yapının adı
İnşa yılı / inşa dönemi
Hangi uygarlık veya devlet tarafından yapıldığı
Yapının işlevi
Görsel mantık:
Önce parşömen üzerinde Türkçe etiketli mürekkep eskizi
Yanına el yazısıyla inşa tarihi
Ardından yapının parşömenden çıkarak tam 3D hale dönüşmesi
• Tarihsel Katmanlar & Eski Uygarlıklar
Şehirde yaşamış uygarlıklar ve imparatorluklar:
Antik dönem
Roma
Bizans
İslam / Osmanlı
Modern Cumhuriyet dönemi
Görsel sunum:
Mürekkep çizimleri → yarı 3D kalıntılar → mimari fragmanlar
(Sütunlar, surlar, kapılar, ibadet yapıları, limanlar)
• Kırılma Anları & Önemli Tarihler — KRONOLOJİK ZORUNLULUK
Şehrin kaderini değiştiren olaylar net tarihlerle birlikte gösterilmelidir.
Örnek türler:
Fetihler
Yıkımlar
Yeniden inşalar
Başkent oluşu
Ticaret yolu değişimleri
Modernleşme adımları
Sunum:
Oklar, zaman çizgileri, tarih damgaları
Kırmızı mürekkeple vurgulanan dönüm noktaları
Türkçe açıklamalı el yazısı notlar
• Günümüz Şehri — MANDATORY FULL 3D
Şehrin bugünkü simgeleri:
Köprüler
Kuleler
Silüet
Modern yapılar
Kamusal alanlar
Kurallar:
Önce parşömen eskizi
Ardından tamamen hacimli, gerçekçi 3D dönüşüm
Taş, metal, cam, beton yüzeyler fiziksel olarak doğru olmalı
Aynı ışık, ölçek ve perspektif kullanılmalı
Düz ikonlar veya poster stili KESİNLİKLE YASAK
• Kültürel Hafıza & Simgesel Anlam
İnançlar
Ticaret
Sanat
Günlük yaşam
Kolektif bilinç
Görsel anlatım:
Simgesel nesneler
Dokular
Türkçe açıklamalı el yazıları
• Mimari & Sanatsal Doku Notları
Yapı teknikleri
Taş işçiliği
Süsleme dili
Dönemsel mimari farklar
Sunum:
Müze etiketi estetiğinde notlar
Eskiz defteri çizimleri
Diyagram bindirmeleri
Visual Continuity Rule
Tüm mürekkep çizgileri ve Türkçe yazılar:
Taşa
Metale
Cam yapılara
Sokaklara ve anıtlara
Gözle takip edilebilir şekilde dönüşmelidir.
Parşömenle bağ KESİNTİYE UĞRAMAMALIDIR.
Visual Effects & Atmosphere
Eskitilmiş parşömen dokusu
Mürekkep taşmaları
Yırtık kenarlar
Kırmızı balmumu mühürler
Arşiv damgaları
Toz parçacıkları
Hafif sis ve katmanlı derinlik
Lighting
Epik golden-hour sinematik ışık
Antik, tarihsel ve modern katmanları tek bir dramatik atmosferde birleştiren aydınlatma
Technical Specifications
8K resolution
Cinematic depth of field
Unreal Engine 5 render
Museum-quality realism
Grand scale
Ultra-detailed textures

**作者**: [@ai.gezgini](https://x.com/ai_gezgini)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/ai_gezgini/status/2000590170635079984)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251216/art-of-transforming-movie-props-into-miniature-scenes-1.jpg" width="500" alt="电影道具迷你舞台（场景）转化的艺术">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251216/art-of-transforming-movie-props-into-miniature-scenes-2.jpg" width="500" alt="电影道具迷你舞台（场景）转化的艺术">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251216/art-of-transforming-movie-props-into-miniature-scenes-3.jpg" width="500" alt="电影道具迷你舞台（场景）转化的艺术">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251216/art-of-transforming-movie-props-into-miniature-scenes-4.jpg" width="500" alt="电影道具迷你舞台（场景）转化的艺术">

```
Filmlerin ikonik araçlarını minyatür sahneye (diorama) dönüştürmek artık çok kolay 🎬
Nano Banana Pro + basit bir prompt yeterli.
Hayal ettiğini sahneye dönüştürmek birkaç satır 🚀
Millenium Falcon için Prompt (tüm promptlar ALT kısmında)
👇
Millennium Falcon’un yer aldığı yakın plan bir masaüstü uzay gemisi dioraması. Fotoğraf, gemiye hafif yukarıdan 3/4 açıyla bakıyor. El yapımı minyatür model, ana gövdeyi ve çevresindeki küçük hangar alanını kadrajın büyük kısmında gösteriyor. Geminin bir yüzü kesit şeklinde açık; iç katmanlar net biçimde görülüyor.
İç mekânda kokpit, yaşam alanı, dinlenme odaları, koridorlar ve makine dairesi kat kat detaylandırılmış; minyatür kontrol panelleri, koltuklar, kablolar ve Star Wars’a özgü endüstriyel detaylar yer alıyor. Dış kısımda uzay limanı platformu, servis araçları, sandıklar ve teknik ekipmanlar bulunuyor.
İçeride ve dışarıda Han Solo, Chewbacca, mürettebat ve bazı droid figürleri mevcut; figürler net ama diorama ölçeğinde. Sığ alan derinliği; ön plan net, arka plan yumuşak flu. Hafif sıcak, sinematik hangar ışığı; yüksek detaylı, stüdyo çekimi bilim kurgu dioraması, ultra gerçekçi.
```

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/one-piece-style-devil-fruit-ability-transformation-1.jpg" width="500" alt="One Piece風デビルフード能力者変身">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/one-piece-style-devil-fruit-ability-transformation-3.jpg" width="500" alt="One Piece風デビルフード能力者変身">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/one-piece-style-devil-fruit-ability-transformation-4.jpg" width="500" alt="One Piece風デビルフード能力者変身">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/one-piece-style-devil-fruit-ability-transformation-5.jpg" width="500" alt="One Piece風デビルフード能力者変身">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/one-piece-style-devil-fruit-ability-transformation-6.jpg" width="500" alt="One Piece風デビルフード能力者変身">

```json
GM!
One Pieceの悪魔の実の名前を入れると、その実の能力者になれるnanobananaのPromptです。
&lt;&lt;DEVIL FRUIT NAME&gt;&gt;に悪魔の実の名前を入れて下さい。実の名前は日本語でも英語でも大丈夫でした😃
Promptはコメントに記載します。
#nanobanana2 https://t.co/645RY7a8yT
最初の<<DEVIL FRUIT NAME>>に悪魔の実の名前を入れて下さい😃
{
  "version": "1.0",
  "description": "Transform a real person in a photo into a One Piece-style Devil Fruit ability user: dynamic pose, dramatic camera angle, ability-specific SFX, and a photorealistic manifestation of the specified Devil Fruit’s power.",
  "variables": {
    "DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "<<DEVIL FRUIT NAME>>",
      "description": "The canonical Devil Fruit name whose ability should be interpreted and applied to the subject (e.g., Gum-Gum Fruit, Flame-Flame Fruit, Ice-Ice Fruit, Sand-Sand Fruit, Rumble-Rumble Fruit, Flower-Flower Fruit, Dark-Dark Fruit, Paw-Paw Fruit, etc.)."
    }
  },
  "steps": [
    {
      "name": "DEVIL_FRUIT_ABILITY_EDIT",
      "goal": "Apply a dynamic One Piece-style pose, dramatic camera angle, ability-specific manga SFX, and a photorealistic manifestation of the specified Devil Fruit’s ability.",
      "instructions": "Use the uploaded photo as the base.\n\nKeep the person photorealistic (eyes, face, skin texture, hair, makeup). Do NOT convert the scene into manga. Do NOT replace the background.\n\n=====================================\nDEVIL FRUIT ABILITY TRANSFORMATION\n=====================================\nInsert your Devil Fruit name here: [DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME]\n\nInterpret the canon ability of [DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME] realistically and apply it to the body or surrounding environment. The effect must look like a live-action One Piece movie.\n\nExamples:\n- Gum-Gum Fruit: stretched limbs, elastic skin, tension folds, rubber reflection\n- Flame-Flame Fruit: realistic flames, heat distortion, warm illumination\n- Ice-Ice Fruit: frost buildup, ice crystals, cold vapor\n- Rumble-Rumble Fruit: lightning arcs, photoreal sparks\n- Sand-Sand Fruit: sand disintegration, sandstorm motion\n- Flower-Flower Fruit: photoreal arms blooming from surfaces\n- Paw-Paw Fruit: shockwave compression ripples\n- Dark-Dark Fruit: gravitational distortion, dark smoke tendrils\n\nRules:\n- The face must remain recognizable.\n- Effects must integrate into real lighting and shadows.\n- No cartoon filters — supernatural physics must look real.\n\n=====================================\nONE PIECE-STYLE POSE TRANSFORMATION\n=====================================\nRepose the body into a dramatic battle pose:\n- wide stance, strong dynamic gestures\n- stretched arm for Gum-Gum, open palm for shockwave, ignition stance for flame, elemental charge-up for logias, etc.\n- clothing should deform realistically\n\n=====================================\nEXTREME CAMERA ANGLES\n=====================================\nChoose one at random:\n- ultra low-angle\n- ultra high-angle\n- 20–24mm wide angle\n- 14mm super-wide distortion\n- fisheye\n- Dutch tilt\n- forced perspective (hand reaching toward lens)\n- telephoto compression (85–135mm)\n\n=====================================\nABILITY-SPECIFIC MANGA SFX (INK LINE ART)\n=====================================\nAutomatically choose the most appropriate SFX based on [DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME].\nUse ONLY One Piece-style onomatopoeia.\n\nWhen generating SFX, follow these rules:\n- pure black ink line art (no gradients)\n- placed behind or beside the character\n- must NOT cover the face\n\nUse the SFX set that matches the ability theme:\n\n=== SFX SELECTION LOGIC ===\nIf [DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME] contains:\n\n- \"Gum-Gum\" → Use: 「ドン!!!」, 「バキィ!!」, 「ゴムッ!!」, 「ブンッ!!」\n- \"Flame-Flame\" → Use: 「メラメラ…」, 「ボッ!!」, 「ゴォォ!!」, 「ドン!!!」\n- \"Ice-Ice\" → Use: 「ヒエェェ…」, 「パキパキ!!」, 「スッ…」\n- \"Rumble-Rumble\" → Use: 「ビリビリッ!!」, 「ズドン!!」, 「ゴロゴロ…」\n- \"Sand-Sand\" → Use: 「サラサラ…」, 「ザザザッ!!」, 「ドン!!」\n- \"Flower-Flower\" → Use: 「パッ!!」, 「ボンッ!!」\n- \"Dark-Dark\" → Use: 「ズズズ…」, 「ゴゴゴゴ…」, 「ドン…!!」\n- \"Paw-Paw\" → Use: 「バシュッ!!」, 「ドン!!」, 「ボフッ!!」\n- otherwise (unknown fruit) → Use: 「ドン!!!」, 「ゴゴゴゴ…」 (universal SFX)\n\n=====================================\nOPTIONAL MANGA LINES\n=====================================\nAdd subtle speed lines, impact lines, or depth lines, but keep the real background visible.\n\n=====================================\nFINAL GOAL\n=====================================\nCreate a photorealistic action image where:\n- The person stays realistic\n- The camera angle is dramatic\n- The pose is dynamic\n- The Devil Fruit ability is manifested photorealistically\n- Ability-appropriate SFX appear as ink line art around them\n\nFinal result must look like \"A real photograph capturing a live-action One Piece Devil Fruit battle moment.\"\n"
    }
  ],
  "final_goal": "Produce a single photorealistic One Piece-style image where the person in the uploaded photo is dynamically posed and visually affected by the real-world manifestation of the chosen Devil Fruit [DEVIL_FRUIT_NAME], with ability-specific SFX."
}
```

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/thread/1998387008092381617)

```
Z-image入れてみました。上段ZIT。下段Qwen。
かなり似てますね。Qwenの方が何となく好きですけれど、ZITの速さは凄いです。
青赤加工はnanobananaです。Promptはコメントに入れておきます😃
#ZImage_Turbo #nanobanana https://t.co/qq3dir9Dkp
Apply an artistic red–blue double-exposure effect using two poses of the same woman. Keep the base layer as the original pose, and generate a second pose where her head angle, facial direction, or expression is slightly different, as if captured a moment earlier or later. Color the second pose in red, the base pose in cyan, and offset the layers to create a clean ghosting effect. Preserve skin texture, tattoos, and contrast while keeping the background minimal.
```

### [乔乔风格摆姿势](https://aiart.pics/prompt/jojo-style-pose-transformation)

**作者**: [@AI Girl's Photo Studio](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/status/1994374306327847341)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/jojo-style-pose-transformation-1.jpg" width="500" alt="乔乔风格摆姿势">

```
◆JOJO立ち　アングル
Use the uploaded photo as the base.
Keep the person’s **face, eyes, hairstyle, makeup, outfit, and overall identity** clearly recognizable and photorealistic.
Do NOT turn the whole image into a drawing.
Do NOT replace or redraw the background; only transform the perspective as needed.
===================================================
TRANSFORM THE POSE — EXTREME “JOJO-STYLE” POSES
===================================================
Repose the body into a **randomized, exaggerated JoJo-style pose**, pushing the limits of human flexibility:
- extreme torso twist, strong contrapposto
- head tilt with dramatic confidence
- one hand framing the face, one arm extended or arched
- bold leg positions (crossed, wide stance, pointed toes)
The pose must be:
- anatomically plausible but exaggerated like JoJo
- stylish, flamboyant, theatrical
Maintain realistic lighting and natural cloth deformation.
===================================================
APPLY EXTREME CAMERA ANGLES (RANDOM EACH TIME)
===================================================
Transform the camera viewpoint to create striking JoJo-style drama:
Choose **one random angle** from the following list for each generation:
- **Ultra low-angle (“仰ぎ見”) shot**: camera near the ground looking upward
- **Ultra high-angle (“見下ろし”) shot**: camera directly above looking down
- **Dynamic wide-angle (20–24mm)**: strong perspective distortion
- **Super wide-angle (14mm)** for extreme depth & stretched limbs
- **Fisheye lens effect** with curved perspective lines
- **Dutch-angle (tilted horizon)** for manga-like tension
- **Close-up with forced perspective**: large foreground hand reaching toward the camera
- **Long-lens compression (85–135mm)** but still JoJo dramatic
Rules:
- The face must remain recognizable and photorealistic in the new angle.
- The background may be warped to match the new perspective, but must remain the same scene.
- No cartoon effects on the person themselves.
===================================================
ADD MANGA-STYLE SFX (JOJO ONOMATOPEIA)
===================================================
Add dramatic Japanese SFX in bold black-and-white ink lines:
- 「ゴゴゴゴゴ…」
- 「ドドドドド…」
- 「ズキューーーン！」
- 「バァーーーン！！」
- 「メメタァ！」
- 「ガオンッ！」
Place them:
- floating behind the person
- along the sides of the pose
- integrated with the new camera angle perspective
Do NOT cover the person’s face.
===================================================
OPTIONAL MANGA LINES
===================================================
Add subtle JoJo-style:
- speed lines
- radiating impact lines
- perspective shock lines
But keep the original background visible through them.
===================================================
FINAL GOAL
===================================================
Create a realistic photo where:
- the person remains fully recognizable,
- their body is transformed into a bold, dramatic JoJo-style pose,
- the camera angle is extreme and cinematic (low-angle, high-angle, fisheye, wide-angle, etc.),
- powerful manga SFX surround them in true JoJo fashion.
The image should feel like a **JoJo splash page happening inside a real photograph**.
```

### [使用NanoBanana创建角度和手足特写Prompt：打造有深度感的动态图像](https://aiart.pics/prompt/using-nanobanana-to-create-angle-and-hand-foot-close-up-prompt)

**作者**: [@AI Girl's Photo Studio](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/status/1997137582258639070)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/using-nanobanana-to-create-angle-and-hand-foot-close-up-prompt-1.jpg" width="500" alt="使用NanoBanana创建角度和手足特写Prompt：打造有深度感的动态图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/using-nanobanana-to-create-angle-and-hand-foot-close-up-prompt-2.jpg" width="500" alt="使用NanoBanana创建角度和手足特写Prompt：打造有深度感的动态图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/using-nanobanana-to-create-angle-and-hand-foot-close-up-prompt-3.jpg" width="500" alt="使用NanoBanana创建角度和手足特写Prompt：打造有深度感的动态图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/using-nanobanana-to-create-angle-and-hand-foot-close-up-prompt-4.jpg" width="500" alt="使用NanoBanana创建角度和手足特写Prompt：打造有深度感的动态图像">

```
一番最後の [Prompt for original image] の部分に画像生成に使用した Prompt を入れると一貫性が増します。不要な場合は 3 行削ってしまっても大丈夫です。
---
Extreme wide-angle perspective and dynamic pose remix edit.
This is an EDIT of the original image, not a new character.
Use the original image as a strict reference for:
– the person’s identity, hairstyle, and overall fashion style,
– the general type of background and location (same street, same room, same beach, same kind of architecture, etc.).
You are allowed to completely change the camera position, angle, and pose, but you must keep the scene in the SAME location and keep the SAME person and outfit design.
Camera and perspective:
– Use an ultra wide-angle or fisheye feeling lens (around 12–18mm full-frame look).
– The camera angle MUST change significantly from the original: use dramatic angles such as
・worm’s-eye view from directly below looking up,
・bird’s-eye view from directly above looking down,
・very low angle from the ground,
・high angle from above,
・tilted Dutch angles.
– Always create strong foreshortening: body parts close to the lens look huge, while the rest of the body falls away in perspective.
– The final result must look like a bold fashion or street photo, fully photorealistic, not illustration or anime.
Background consistency:
– Keep the same location as the original image: same street, same bridge, same room, same studio, same beach, same general structures and materials.
– Do NOT replace the background with a completely different place.
– Because the camera angle changes, it is allowed and expected that different parts of the environment become visible.
– When new areas appear, extend the original environment logically (same buildings, fences, road markings, walls, colors, materials, lighting style), as if the camera moved within the same place.
Body parts near the lens (1–2 parts, sometimes 3):
– In each edit, choose ONE or TWO main body parts to be extremely close to the lens (sometimes even THREE in more complex poses).
– Vary them from image to image, do NOT always use the same body part.
– Allowed near-the-lens parts include:
・one or both hands / fingers reaching toward the camera,
・one or both feet / shoes / boots near the lens,
・knees or thighs,
・face very close to the lens,
・shoulders or chest close to the lens in a leaning pose.
– The chosen body parts should come extremely close to the lens, almost touching it, with visible skin texture, fabric texture, and realistic wide-angle distortion.
Pose and overall body (complex and varied):
– Create strong, cool, dynamic poses that match the extreme perspective.
– Randomly use different pose types, including:
・standing with one leg or one arm reaching toward the camera,
・crouching or squatting low to the ground,
・sitting on the floor or on objects,
・lying on the ground with legs or feet toward the lens,
・leaning forward aggressively toward the camera,
・twisting the body, crossing legs, or arching the back for more dynamic lines.
– Allow complex poses where:
・both hands are near the lens forming shapes (peace signs, triangles, frames, pointing toward the viewer),
・both feet are toward the lens,
・one hand and one foot are both large in the foreground,
・the face is close to the lens while hands or feet are also visible in perspective.
– Maintain believable anatomy even with extreme foreshortening.
Angle and attitude (randomized):
– Randomize camera angle and orientation (up, down, side, Dutch tilt) while keeping the composition visually balanced and powerful.
– Keep the vibe cool, confident, and fashion/editorial or street style, depending on the original outfit.
– Facial expressions can vary (serious, playful, confident, mysterious), but must still look like the same person.
Lighting and rendering:
– Keep the general time of day and lighting mood similar to the original (night vs day, indoor vs outdoor, soft vs hard light), but you may enhance contrast and color to make the image punchy and dramatic.
– Maintain realistic shadows and contact points with the ground or floor.
– High-resolution, sharp details with clear skin texture, fabric weave, and material highlights.
Variation and randomness:
– Each edit should look noticeably different from the original image and from other edits, with different:
・camera angles,
・pose types,
・which body parts are closest to the lens,
・orientation (straight, tilted, from above, from below).
– Avoid repeating the exact same single-foot-close-up composition; produce a wide variety of dynamic poses and angles.
Strict rules:
– Do NOT change the person into someone else.
– Do NOT change the outfit type; only restyle it through pose, perspective, and small natural movement of clothing.
– Do NOT move the scene to a completely different location; always stay in a plausible extension of the original place.
– Do NOT add text, logos, watermarks, or graphic design elements.
– Do NOT switch to painting, illustration, or anime style; keep it photorealistic.
Overall:
Transform the original photo into a dramatic, photorealistic, ultra wide-angle shot with an extreme camera angle (including views from directly below or above), where one or more body parts are right next to the lens and look huge, the rest of the body recedes in perspective, and the same person strikes a stylish, complex, powerful pose in a consistent, expanded version of the original environment.
Also, below is the prompt for generating the original image. Please use it as a reference.
[Prompt for original image]
#nanobanana2
```

### [原始图像的极端广角视角和动态姿态混剪编辑](https://aiart.pics/prompt/extreme-wide-angle-perspective-and-dynamic-pose-remix-edit-of-the-original-image)

```
一番最後の[Prompt for original image]の部分に画像生成に使用したPromptを入れると一貫性が増します。不要な場合は3行削ってしまっても大丈夫です。
---
Extreme wide-angle perspective and dynamic pose remix edit.

– the person’s identity, hairstyle, and overall fashion style,
– the general type of background and location (same street, same room, same beach, same kind of architecture, etc.).

– Use an ultra wide-angle or fisheye feeling lens (around 12–18mm full-frame look).

• worm’s-eye view from directly below looking up,
• bird’s-eye view from directly above looking down,
• very low angle from the ground,
• high angle from above,
• tilted Dutch angles.

• one or both hands / fingers reaching toward the camera,
• one or both feet / shoes / boots near the lens,
• knees or thighs,
• face very close to the lens,

• standing with one leg or one arm reaching toward the camera,
• crouching or squatting low to the ground,
• sitting on the floor or on objects,
• lying on the ground with legs or feet toward the lens,
• leaning forward aggressively toward the camera,
• twisting the body, crossing legs, or arching the back for more dynamic lines.
– Allow complex poses where:
• both hands are near the lens forming shapes (peace signs, triangles, frames, pointing toward the viewer),
• both feet are toward the lens,
• one hand and one foot are both large in the foreground,
• the face is close to the lens while hands or feet are also visible in perspective.
– Maintain believable anatomy even with extreme foreshortening.

– Randomize camera angle and orientation (up, down, side, Dutch tilt) while keeping the composition visually balanced and powerful.

– Keep the general time of day and lighting mood similar to the original (night vs day, indoor vs outdoor, soft vs hard light), but you may enhance contrast and color to make the image punchy and dramatic.
– Maintain realistic shadows and contact points with the ground or floor.
– High-resolution, sharp details with clear skin texture, fabric weave, and material highlights.

– Each edit should look noticeably different from the original image and from other edits, with different:
• camera angles,
• pose types,
• which body parts are closest to the lens,
• orientation (straight, tilted, from above, from below).
– Avoid repeating the exact same single-foot-close-up composition; produce a wide variety of dynamic poses and angles.

– Do NOT change the person into someone else.
– Do NOT change the outfit type; only restyle it through pose, perspective, and small natural movement of clothing.
– Do NOT move the scene to a completely different location; always stay in a plausible extension of the original place.
– Do NOT add text, logos, watermarks, or graphic design elements.
– Do NOT switch to painting, illustration, or anime style; keep it photorealistic.

### [透明文字服制作方法：nanobanana Ver1.2教程](https://aiart.pics/prompt/transparent-typographic-garment-nanobanana-ver1-2-guide)

**作者**: [@AI Girl's Photo Studio](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/thread/1994725357912744432)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/transparent-typographic-garment-nanobanana-ver1-2-guide-1.jpg" width="500" alt="透明文字服制作方法：nanobanana Ver1.2教程">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/transparent-typographic-garment-nanobanana-ver1-2-guide-2.jpg" width="500" alt="透明文字服制作方法：nanobanana Ver1.2教程">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/transparent-typographic-garment-nanobanana-ver1-2-guide-3.jpg" width="500" alt="透明文字服制作方法：nanobanana Ver1.2教程">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251207/transparent-typographic-garment-nanobanana-ver1-2-guide-4.jpg" width="500" alt="透明文字服制作方法：nanobanana Ver1.2教程">

```json
服を文字に変えて透過させる件、Hailuo以外のnanobananaでも精度高くする方法を探ってました。どうも服の色を抽出して文字色に置き換えるところがなかなか難しいらしく、手間ですが、服の色をカラーコードで指定するようにしたら精度が上がった気がします。ただ、肉体は透過してくれないようで素肌に文字着るようになってしまいました。
無料のnanobananaだと添付の通り2回エラーになってしまったので、3回しか回せてないですが、2回は成功。現状のVer1.2としてコメントにPromptを記載します。
良かったら皆さんもちゃんと動くか検証してみて下さい。文字色とYOUR TEXTを変えられます。
ちゃんと動きますように。
#nanobanana2 #qwen
{
  "version": "1.2",
  "description": "Photorealistic removal of clothing and replacement with a transparent typographic garment made only of flat-colored letters, using a clean-plate background and compositing. Text colors are explicitly provided as variables (no automatic color sampling).",
  "variables": {
    "YOUR_TEXT": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "<<YOUR_TEXT>>",
      "description": "The text used to build the typographic garment. It will repeat, warp, rotate and fill the clothing silhouette."
    },
    "GARMENT_MAIN_COLOR": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "#7fffd4",
      "description": "Hex color for all garment letters if there is only one clothing piece (e.g., a dress or hoodie). Example: #FFFFFF for white, #FF7AA5 for pink."
    },
    "GARMENT_TOP_COLOR": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "#7fffd4",
      "description": "Hex color for the top garment letters (e.g., hoodie/shirt). Only used if there is a separate top."
    },
    "GARMENT_BOTTOM_COLOR": {
      "type": "string",
      "value": "#000000",
      "description": "Hex color for the bottom garment letters (e.g., shorts/skirt/pants). Only used if there is a separate bottom."
    }
  },
  "steps": [
    {
      "name": "STEP_1_CLEAN_PLATE_BACKGROUND",
      "goal": "Remove the person completely and reconstruct a perfectly photorealistic background as if the person was never there.",
      "instructions": "Using the uploaded photo, completely remove the person from the image.\n\nInpaint the area they occupied, reconstructing the background behind them with perfect photorealism that matches the original environment.\nExtend all environmental elements naturally — ground, floor tiles, asphalt, buildings, cars, signs, sky, trees, walls, indoor furniture, or any other background objects depending on the scene.\nThere must be no remaining silhouette, no blur, no cloning patterns, and no smudging.\nThe result of this step must look like the original photo was taken with no person in it at all."
    },
    {
      "name": "STEP_2_COLORED_TYPOGRAPHIC_GARMENT_LAYER",
      "goal": "On the original photo, replace all clothing with a flat-colored typographic garment over chroma green, with full transparency between letters.",
      "instructions": "Return to the original photo with the person present.\n\nElements that must remain unchanged:\n- keep the face, skin, eyes, hair, makeup, and body shape completely photorealistic\n- keep the person’s pose, limb positions, and the original lighting and shadows on the skin\n- keep all non-clothing objects such as bags, accessories, jewelry, and props untouched\n- keep the background intact\n\nModify ONLY the clothing:\n- remove all original fabric information from every garment: delete texture, folds, seams, wrinkles, shading, logos, and printed graphics\n- the clothing must no longer look like fabric in any way\n\nReplace each garment area with a new garment made only of flat hand-drawn text.\n\nTEXT CONTENT:\nUse the following content as the base text for the garment:\n[YOUR_TEXT]\nRepeat, rotate, scale, warp, and curve these letters as needed so they densely fill the entire silhouette of each garment.\n\nCOLOR RULES (NO SAMPLING, USE PROVIDED COLORS):\n- If there is only one continuous garment (for example, a single dress or one hoodie), use GARMENT_MAIN_COLOR as the flat fill color for all letters.\n- If there is a clearly separate top and bottom:\n  * use GARMENT_TOP_COLOR for all letters in the top garment area (hoodie, shirt, jacket, etc.)\n  * use GARMENT_BOTTOM_COLOR for all letters in the bottom garment area (shorts, skirt, pants, etc.)\n- Letters must be filled with a single flat color per garment region.\n- Absolutely no gradients, no highlights, no shadows, no fabric textures may be added to the letters.\n\nTypography style:\n- letters must appear as flat graphic shapes (not fabric)\n- slightly irregular stroke width is allowed so they feel hand-drawn\n- letters may curve to follow the body’s form, but color must remain perfectly flat.\n\nTransparency and chroma key rules:\n- every area inside the garment that is NOT covered by a letter must be pure chroma green (RGB 0,255,0)\n- do NOT leave any gray, black, or residual fabric color under or between letters\n- there must be absolutely no shading, folds, highlights, or fabric texture under the letters\n- the result of this step should look like the person is wearing a garment made of a dense mesh of flat-colored letters floating over solid chroma green, with no other fill color present."
    },
    {
      "name": "STEP_3_FINAL_COMPOSITE_WITH_CLEAN_PLATE",
      "goal": "Composite the typographic garment person over the clean background so the real environment shows through the gaps between letters.",
      "instructions": "Take the result from STEP 2 and key out all pure chroma green (RGB 0,255,0) so that these regions become fully transparent.\n\nThen place this keyed image of the person with the typographic garment onto the clean-plate background produced in STEP 1.\nAlign the person perfectly with their original position and camera perspective so that the integration is seamless.\n\nThrough all gaps between the letters, the reconstructed real background from STEP 1 must be clearly visible.\nDo not introduce any artificial flat color where transparency should reveal the environment.\n\nRecalculate natural cast shadows from the person onto the ground, walls, or nearby objects, but base the shadow shape on the current body and garment silhouette, not on the original clothing.\nMatch light direction, softness, intensity, and noise/grain with the original photo.\n\nThe final composite must be fully photorealistic:\n- the person remains realistic and unchanged except for the garment\n- all original fabric, seams, wrinkles, and clothing shadows are gone\n- the garment is now entirely formed by flat colored hand-drawn text\n- the real environment is visible in the transparent gaps between letters\n- there are no green artifacts and no signs of the original clothing."
    }
  ],
  "final_goal": "Produce a single photorealistic image where the person appears to be wearing a garment made only of flat colored letters, with the true scene behind them visible through all gaps between letters, and no trace of the original clothing or its shadows."
}
ちなみに、Hailuoのnanobanana2はhailuoのエージェント経由で処理されるので、Promptで3stepに分かれていると以下のように右側のAgentが実際に3回に分けて画像生成します。1つ目で女性を消して背景を取り、2つ目で服をクロマキー処理して、服色に合わせた文字を埋め、3つ目でクロマキー処理した緑の部分を透過させて合成するという感じに実際やります。
他のNanobanana2やNanobanana Proもみんなこういうエージェントっぽい処理をするものだと思ってましたが、Hailuoが特殊なのですね…。
