### [今日发布了一篇将衣服文字化的帖子，但那只是第一步。](https://aiart.pics/prompt/today-post-text-clothing-first-step)

**作者**: [@AI Girl's Photo Studio](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/status/1994000421652963625)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251205/today-post-text-clothing-first-step-1.jpg" width="500" alt="今日发布了一篇将衣服文字化的帖子，但那只是第一步。">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251205/today-post-text-clothing-first-step-2.jpg" width="500" alt="今日发布了一篇将衣服文字化的帖子，但那只是第一步。">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251205/today-post-text-clothing-first-step-3.jpg" width="500" alt="今日发布了一篇将衣服文字化的帖子，但那只是第一步。">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251205/today-post-text-clothing-first-step-4.jpg" width="500" alt="今日发布了一篇将衣服文字化的帖子，但那只是第一步。">

```
今朝、服を文字に変える投稿をしましたが、あれは実は1stステップでした。服を文字に変える場合、文字と文字の隙間ができますが、その隙間には元画像には写っていない背景を透過する必要があります。
朝の投稿は背景の白が入ればいいだけなので、比較的出しやすいのですが、街中のショットの場合、画像に合わせた背景も埋めてもらう必要があります。
Hailuo、Higgs、Nano Banana Proで同じPromptを試したところ、Hailuoが一番綺麗に生成できる確率が高かったです。Hailuoの場合、AIエージェントが画像を元にPromptを書き換えるので、精度が上がるようです。Higgosも表に見えないけれど、多分Prompt補正されているのかな、って思っています。
成功率はHailuoで半々くらいでしょうか。失敗すると最後の画像のようになります。これはこれでアリなのかもしれませんけれど😃
Promptはコメントに。[YOUR_TEXT]に服にしたい文字を入れます。
1枚目は一律白文字にするパターンですが、コメントに記載のものは服のパーツに合わせて文字色を変えます。
#nanobanana2 #qwen
```

### [在人物周围添加糖果怪兽](https://aiart.pics/prompt/add-candy-monsters-around-character)

**作者**: [@AI Girl's Photo Studio](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_GIRL_DESIGN/status/1993243344932413597)

```
Use the uploaded photo. \nDo NOT alter the person’s real appearance — keep the person’s face, body, clothing, colors, and texture completely photorealistic. \nDo NOT change the background perspective. \nDo NOT turn the person into a drawing or illustration.\n\nAdd a dense, overloaded layer of pop-style illustrated “sweets monsters” and graphic decorations ONLY around the person (and on top of their clothing if needed), but never on their skin or face.\n\nIllustrated elements:\n- many colorful cartoon monsters with thick black outlines, flat colors, and cute-but-ugly expressions\n- sweets-inspired monsters: bananas, cookies, strawberries, melting chocolate, lollipops, ice cream, oranges, cupcakes, donuts, candy pieces, soda bottles, etc.\n- additional graphic shapes: stars, hearts, arrows, drips, splashes, zigzag lines, exclamation marks, motion lines, sparkles, bubbles, comic-style text shapes (but no real text)\n\nMake the decoration very dense and “busy”:\n- fill the space behind the person with overlapping sweets monsters and shapes\n- add monsters peeking from behind the shoulders, around the bag, at the person’s feet, and near the head\n- allow some monsters and shapes to overlap the clothing and accessories (shirt, shorts, bag, shoes), but keep the skin of the face, arms, and legs photorealistic and visible\n- use multiple layers of illustrations in front of and behind the person to create depth\n- add glowing outlines, small white dots, and speed lines around the person to emphasize energy\n\nColor and style:\n- use a vivid, neon-like color palette (hot pink, yellow, cyan, lime, orange, purple, turquoise)\n- keep all illustrated elements flat and graphic with clean edges and bold outlines\n- ensure shadows and overlap suggest interaction with the real person (e.g., slight shadows on clothing where monsters touch)\n\nOverall goal:\nCreate a highly decorated, maximalist pop-art scene where the real person stands in the middle, surrounded and wrapped by a chaotic crowd of playful sweets monsters and graphic doodles, while the person remains clearly photorealistic.
请使用已上传的照片。\n不要改变人物的真实外貌——保持人物的脸部、身体、衣服、颜色和纹理完全逼真。\n请勿改变背景视角。\n请勿将人物形象转化为绘画或插图。\n\n在人物周围（必要时可以贴在衣服上）添加一层厚重的、过多的流行风格插画“糖果怪兽”和图形装饰，但绝不能贴在皮肤或脸上。\n\n图示元素：\n- 许多色彩鲜艳的卡通怪物，轮廓线粗黑，色彩扁平，表情可爱又丑陋。\n- 以甜食为灵感的怪物：香蕉、饼干、草莓、融化的巧克力、棒棒糖、冰淇淋、橙子、纸杯蛋糕、甜甜圈、糖果块、汽水瓶等等。\n- 其他图形形状：星星、心形、箭头、水滴、飞溅、锯齿线、感叹号、动态线条、闪光、气泡、漫画风格的文字形状（但不能包含实际文字）\n\n装饰要非常密集、繁复：\n- 用重叠的糖果怪兽和形状填满人身后的空间\n- 添加一些怪物，它们会从肩膀后面、包周围、人的脚边和头部附近探出头来。\n允许部分怪物和形状与服装及配饰（衬衫、短裤、包、鞋子）重叠，但保持面部、手臂和腿部的皮肤逼真可见。\n- 在人物前后使用多层插图来营造景深。\n- 在人物周围添加发光轮廓、小白点和速度线，以强调能量。\n\n颜色和款式：\n- 使用鲜艳的霓虹色系调色板（亮粉色、黄色、青色、酸橙色、橙色、紫色、蓝绿色）\n- 保持所有插图元素扁平化、图形化，边缘清晰，轮廓粗犷。\n- 确保阴影和重叠能够暗示与真人的互动（例如，怪物触碰衣服时在衣服上留下淡淡的阴影）\n\n总体目标：\n创作一幅装饰华丽、极繁主义的波普艺术场景，真人站在场景中央，被一群嬉戏玩闹的糖果怪兽和涂鸦图形包围，而真人则保持清晰的写实风格。
```

## Kei🍤衣装本舗

### [使用Nano Banana制作虚构Vtuber直播画面](https://aiart.pics/prompt/creating-a-fictional-vtuber-streaming-screen-with-nano-banana)

**作者**: [@Kei🍤衣装本舗](https://x.com/AI_Kei75)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AI_Kei75/status/1967490141578236329)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/creating-a-fictional-vtuber-streaming-screen-with-nano-banana-1.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana制作虚构Vtuber直播画面">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/creating-a-fictional-vtuber-streaming-screen-with-nano-banana-2.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana制作虚构Vtuber直播画面">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/creating-a-fictional-vtuber-streaming-screen-with-nano-banana-3.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana制作虚构Vtuber直播画面">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/creating-a-fictional-vtuber-streaming-screen-with-nano-banana-4.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana制作虚构Vtuber直播画面">

```
（検索除外のため再投稿です）
Nano Banana🍌で「Vtuber」を作るためのプロンプトです🐱🎮
１枚目、２枚目：元画像＋Nano Banana＋プロンプトで作成した画像
３枚目、４枚目：元画像
※元画像はアニメ系のほうが好ましいと思われます。
※縦長の画像も作れますが、横長のほうが画面の収まりは良くなります。
※Nano Banana(Gemini 2.5 Flash Image)は「Google AI Studio」等で無料で使えます。
以下、使用したプロンプトです。プロンプトはご自由にお使い下さい💫
Create a fictional Vtuber and their streaming screen using the original image.
The Vtuber's hairstyle and clothing will be faithfully reproduced from the original image.
The Vtuber image will be 2.5D-like, so it is not necessary to perfectly reproduce the style of the original image. A moderate sense of three-dimensionality is also necessary.
The Vtuber's facial expression and pose may be changed from the original image. Have the Vtuber hold a game controller.
Place only the Vtuber's upper body in the bottom right of the screen. Place the streaming screen of the game being played in the center of the screen. Place the chat screen on the left side of the screen.
The screen ratio is set to a larger size for the game screen, and the upper half of the Vtuber's body is displayed smaller.
The background of the original image is completely ignored, as well as the original image pose.
Add a fictional streaming platform and browser UI to the top and bottom of the screen.
The aspect ratio of the generated image is independent of that of the original image.
```

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/create-original-constellations-with-nano-banana-1.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana创作原创星座图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/create-original-constellations-with-nano-banana-2.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana创作原创星座图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/create-original-constellations-with-nano-banana-3.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana创作原创星座图像">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251204/create-original-constellations-with-nano-banana-4.jpg" width="500" alt="使用Nano Banana创作原创星座图像">

```
Nano Banana🍌で「オリジナルの星座」を作るためのプロンプトです♈️♏️♋️
１枚目、２枚目：元画像＋Nano Banana＋プロンプトで作成した画像
３枚目、４枚目：元画像
※元画像はアニメ系、実写系、どちらでも使えます。
※Nano Banana(Gemini 2.5 Flash Image)は「Google AI Studio」等で無料で使えます。
以下、使用したプロンプトです。プロンプトはご自由にお使い下さい💫
Create an image depicting fictional constellations using the original image as a reference.
A photorealistic starry sky. This is maintained even if the original image is anime-style.
People, animals, and objects extracted from the original image are placed transparently against the starry sky background. In this case, the extracted target should be a single motif that is the main theme. Also, only one image should be placed.
The character design, style, and taste of the original image are faithfully reproduced. The background of the original image can be ignored.
An imaginary constellation is created based on the placed motif. This constellation is made up of approximately 5 to 10 stars.
The pose of the original image is analyzed, and the stars belonging to the constellation are appropriately positioned in distinctive parts.
The stars belonging to the constellation are highlighted, and the stars are connected with glowing lines.
```

Create a vertical 9:16 brand design guide poster using the uploaded product image. Adapt the design style to match the product’s niche and visual identity. Structure the poster with clear, elegant sections: (1) Large logo display and safe zone usage, (2) Product mockup centered and highlighted, (3) Primary and secondary color palette swatches with hex codes, (4) Typography guide with heading, subheading, body font samples, and line spacing specs, (5) Iconography or graphic motif examples used by the brand, (6) Image treatment style with sample lifestyle or studio visuals, (7) Grid system or layout rules, (8) Packaging mockups and surface applications, (9) Do’s & Don’ts with annotated visuals. | P09 | BLOOD PROTOCOL | 红/黑/骨白 | 血脉流动/生命汲取/诅咒印记 | 血刃/骨镰/吸血系 |

### 🎨 J. 配色方案
| 协议 | 背景渐变 | 主强调色 | 次强调色 | 状态色 |
|:----:|----------|:--------:|:--------:|:------:|
| P01 HEAVEN | #0d0d0d → #1a1a2e | 金 #ffd700 | 青 #00d4ff | 绿 #00ff88 |
| P02 ENTROPY | #050508 → #1a0a2e | 紫 #9b30ff | 洋红 #ff0080 | 红 #ff2222 |
| P03 VULCAN | #0d0808 → #2e1a0a | 橙 #ff6600 | 红 #ff2200 | 黄 #ffcc00 |
| P04 COSMOS | #020208 → #0a0a1a | 冰蓝 #00d4ff | 极光谱 | 白 #f0f8ff |
| P05 STORM | #0d0d12 → #1a1a2e | 电蓝 #00aaff | 紫 #6666ff | 黄 #ffff00 |

### ⚙️ L. 技术参数
| 参数 | 选项 | 说明 |
|:----:|------|------|
| `--ar` | `16:9` | 标准展示 (推荐) |
| | `21:9` | 超宽电影感 |
| | `4:3` | 传统屏幕 |
| | `9:16` | 竖版单武器 |
| `--stylize` | `280-320` | 写实精密风格 |
| | `320-380` | 平衡风格 (推荐) |
| | `380-450` | 艺术风格化 |
| | `450+` | 极致风格 |
| `--quality` | `2` | 最高品质 (推荐) |
| 渲染描述 | photorealistic hologram | 标准 |
| | crystal-clear projection | 高端 |
| | unstable glitch render | 腐化系 |
| 品质定位 | AAA game UI quality | 游戏风格 |
| | Apple-level design precision | 极简高端 |
| | museum exhibition quality | 收藏展示 |

| P08 | + | bright light, colorful, daylight, warm |
| P09 | + | pure, holy, clean, peaceful, gentle |

## 五、完整示例模板
### 示例：神圣圣剑 (P01 HEAVEN)
```
Premium illustrated modern holographic weapon database spread,
HEAVEN PROTOCOL high-end museum exhibition hall display style.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
LEFT PANEL (55%) · HOLOGRAPHIC WEAPON DISPLAY
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
「DAWNBREAKER ARBITER · 曙光审判者」
MAIN PROJECTION:
Legendary holy greatsword rendered as pristine crystal-clear holographic display,
weapon floating in center of cylindrical hard-light projection field,
slow 360° rotation (3 RPM) with golden divine particles ascending,
projection base: brushed gunmetal platform with concentric light rings,
celestial gold holographic grid with sacred geometry overlay,
divine power readouts fluctuating in projection corners.
HOLOGRAM QUALITIES:
Primary render: Celestial nano-steel with embedded light-circuit channels,
secondary layer: soft cyan wireframe overlay at 20% opacity,
tertiary layer: golden particle aura with ascending holy motes,
projection artifacts: subtle divine shimmer and warm light bloom,
depth effect: Blade appears to radiate sanctity.

## 七、快速使用流程
```
╔═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                     WEAPON CODEX QUICK START                            ║
╠═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                         ║
║   STEP 1 │ 选择协议主题 (P01-P10)                                       ║
║          │ → 确定视觉风格和色彩基调                                     ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 2 │ 匹配展示环境 (E01-E10)                                       ║
║          │ → 确保环境与协议协调                                         ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 3 │ 填入武器基础信息                                             ║
║          │ → 名称 (中英文) / 类型 / 稀有度                              ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 4 │ 配置全息展示                                                 ║
║          │ → 投影容器 / 运动状态 / 动态特效                             ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 5 │ 描述武器细节                                                 ║
║          │ → 各部位材质 + 科技融合描述                                  ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 6 │ 填写浮动标注                                                 ║
║          │ → 材质成分 / 核心输出 / 边缘规格                             ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 7 │ 完善数据面板                                                 ║
║          │ → 战斗属性 / 伤害类型 / 材质分析                             ║
║          │ → 强化槽位 / 特殊能力 / 获取需求                             ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 8 │ 调整技术参数                                                 ║
║          │ → --stylize (参考稀有度表)                                   ║
║          │ → --no (参考排除项表)                                        ║
║          ↓                                                              ║
║   STEP 9 │ 生成 → 评估 → 微调 → 完成                                    ║
║                                                                         ║
╚═════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```
---
## 八、系列一致性锁定
```
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
制作武器系列时，锁定以下参数确保视觉统一：
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🔒 固定项（所有系列武器相同）：
--ar 16:9
--quality 2
--seed [固定种子号]        ← 风格一致性关键
协议主题:    [统一协议]
展示环境:    [统一环境]
投影容器:    [统一形状]
面板布局:    55% / 45%
状态栏格式:  [协议]™ ARMORY DATABASE v[版本]
配色方案:
├─ 背景渐变: [固定]
├─ 主强调色: [固定]
└─ 次强调色: [固定]
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🔄 变化项（每把武器不同）：
武器名称 / 武器类型 / 稀有度
材质描述 / 部位细节
数据数值 / 特殊能力
stylize值 (可在范围内微调)
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
```
---
## 九、协议速配总表
```
╔═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║                          PROTOCOL QUICK MATCH TABLE                               ║
╠═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                                   ║
║  协议    │ 最佳武器类型      │ 推荐环境 │ Stylize │ 核心特效                      ║
║  ────────┼───────────────────┼──────────┼─────────┼─────────────────────────────  ║
║  P01     │ 圣剑/神杖/光明系  │ E01      │ 350-400 │ 金色神圣粒子上升              ║
║  P02     │ 死镰/诅咒刃/暗黑  │ E02      │ 280-330 │ 紫黑腐化故障+虚空裂隙         ║
║  P03     │ 巨斧/战锤/火焰系  │ E03      │ 320-380 │ 橙红热浪扭曲+熔岩流动         ║
║  P04     │ 法杖/星辰刃/寒冰  │ E04      │ 380-450 │ 冰蓝极光+时间冻结             ║
║  P05     │ 战锤/长矛/雷电系  │ E05      │ 320-380 │ 蓝紫电弧+磁场干扰             ║
║  P06     │ 光刃/纳米刀/科技  │ E06      │ 300-350 │ 青洋红相位偏移+现实撕裂       ║
║  P07     │ 长弓/德鲁伊杖    │ E07      │ 350-400 │ 绿金生命脉络+自然粒子         ║
║  P08     │ 匕首/暗杀刃      │ E08      │ 300-350 │ 银紫暗影流动+月光              ║
║  P09     │ 血刃/骨镰        │ E09      │ 280-330 │ 红黑血脉+诅咒符文              ║
║  P10     │ 能量枪/机械臂    │ E06/E10  │ 300-350 │ 银蓝数据流+精密机械           ║
║                                                                                   ║
╚═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```
---
使用建议：
1. **快速开始**: 选择协议 → 复制空白模板 → 填入武器信息
2. **系列制作**: 锁定种子号和协议，只改变武器内容
3. **风格微调**: 在推荐stylize范围内调整以获得最佳效果
4. **排除项**: 务必添加协议专属排除项避免风格冲突
-----------------------------
Part 3 End
All Prompt End.
```

Mythology storybooks are a goldmine for AI monetization right now. 📖💰

Look how it mastered Greek Mythology. Same prompt, different world. Pure magic. 👇
Medusa, Pegasus, Minotaur, and Cyclops
神话故事绘本这个变现赛道，水其实很深。📖✨
很多人以为我这套提示词只能跑《山海经》，那真的太小看它的底层架构了。换个文化背景，希腊神话照样拿捏得死死的。
什么叫“通杀”级别的提示词？看图就懂了。👇
美杜莎，飞马，弥诺陶洛斯，独眼巨人

## 📝 空白速填模板
```
Premium illustrated book spread design, modern infographic bestiary style,
futuristic digital encyclopedia aesthetic with holographic UI elements.
LEFT PANEL (55%):
[______] in [______] pose, materializing from
digital ink-wash simulation with holographic glitch effects.
2D brushwork into 3D [__________材质__________].
BG: Dark slate, hexagonal grid, circuit traces.
Atmos: Data points, holographic rings, [______特效______].

Glassmorphism panels, hexagonal border + [______纹样______].
Header: "[中文] · [English]", seal stamp hologram.
┌─ STATS PANEL ─────────────────┐
│ Element: [____] [__]          │
│ Domain: [____] [__]           │
│ Season: [____] [__]           │
│ Power: [__]% ▰▰▰▰▰▱▱▱▱▱       │
│ Rarity: [___] ★★★★★          │
└───────────────────────────────┘
Data zones: Hexagonal radar, [__] element icon, size comparison, wireframe.
Decor: Corner brackets [____] glow, hexagon clusters, grid overlay.
UNITY: [__________桥接__________] across panels.
Palette: Navy base, [____], [____], cyan, [____] highlights.
8K, Octane, UI/UX quality.

### [服装海报生成指南](https://aiart.pics/prompt/outfit-poster-generation-guidelines)

**作者**: [@大卫叔的AI旅程](https://x.com/aidavid125)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/aidavid125/thread/2004699464255356984)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251227/outfit-poster-generation-guidelines-1.jpg" width="500" alt="服装海报生成指南">

```
很多人都问提示词，提示词评论区见：
Disclaimer: AI-generated content for educational reference only. Not for commercial use. https://t.co/SkRzVs5Pv1
Prompt:
--------------------------
Using the uploaded photo as the sole character reference, generate a vertical outfit poster.
【LAYOUT HARD RULES】
- Must have exactly 6 cards only, 2 rows × 3 columns (3 columns across, 2 rows down)
- Row 1: LOOK 1, 2, 3 | Row 2: LOOK 4, 5, 6
- Prohibited: 9-grid, 3 rows × 2 columns, 2-column layout, extra cards, top header/title
【CANVAS & LAYOUT】
- Vertical 4:5 aspect ratio, background #F7F5F2
- Grid occupies ≥92% of canvas height, bottom margin ≤3%
- Outer margin 2%, spacing 1.5%, strictly aligned
【CARD SPECIFICATIONS】
- White background #FFFFFF, border-radius 5%, stroke 1px #E5E7EB
- Top title bar: height 12%, background #F3F4F6, text color #111827
- Sans-serif font, alignment consistent throughout
【CHARACTER CONSISTENCY】
- All 6 must be the same person in different outfits: same face, same hairstyle, same body proportions, same demeanor
- Prohibited: switching people/changing face/altering gender features/extreme slimming or leg lengthening
【PHOTOGRAPHY QUALITY】
- Master-level studio full-body lookbook, 85mm portrait lens look
- Softbox key light + subtle fill, natural skin texture with light retouching
- Solid seamless background (white/light gray/off-white), no clutter
【UNIFORM CROPPING】
- 4:5 full-body, complete from head to shoes
- Subject centered, height 88%±2%
- Headroom 2-4%, footroom 3-5%, shoes fully visible
- All six shots: consistent camera height/focal length/lighting/pose
【OUTFIT RULES】
- Auto-adapt based on subject age (adult/child)
- Each look ≤3 core items, max 3 colors per outfit, accessories ≤2
- 6 looks distinctly different, but unified style: minimal/clean/polished/easy to recreate
【TITLE SETS】
Adult: Business/Classic → Casual/Weekend → Smart Casual/Evening → Resort/Vacation → Athleisure/Active → Layered/Transitional
Kids: Everyday/Clean → School/Polished → Weekend/Play → Party/Sweet → Active/Sporty → Layered/Cozy
NEGATIVE:
3x3, nine-grid, 9 cards, extra cards, 3 rows x 2 columns, two-column layout, big top header, page title, switching people, changing face, multiple people, lowres, blurry, plastic skin, wide-angle distortion, fisheye, warped body, extreme slimming, long legs effect, outdoor background, textured wall, cut off shoes, half body, adultification, sexy, lingerie, see-through, high heels (kids), heavy makeup (kids), watermark, cropped text
--------------------------
How to use it:
Using uploaded photo, generate a 6-panel outfit poster: strict 2 rows × 3 columns, same person in different outfits, studio full-body shots, 85mm lens look, white cards with title bars, no top header, subject at 88% height from head to shoes, 6 distinct but minimal/polished looks.
```

---

```
House Decoration Design Senario.
爆肝一天，房屋装修场景。以这套中式为例：
对称式布局打造的视觉秩序感，配合吊顶的木格栅线条，将中式传统建筑的骨架完美复刻。最精妙的是光影的处理，暖色侧灯与自然光的交织，让山水背墙成了视觉中心。
博古架、罗汉床、盆景，每一个物件都在诉说东方的韵律。这才是真正的“博古通今”。

Details_CN: "设计细节"
```
---
## 3) 通用负面提示词库（室内设计专用｜TextMode A）
```text
--no lowres, blurry, noise, distorted, cluttered, watermark, amateur, bad lighting
--no misspelled text, gibberish, random characters, illegible text, blurry text, text cut off, text overlap
--no bad perspective, warped walls, crooked lines, wrong proportions, unrealistic scale
--no floating furniture, impossible architecture, physics-defying elements
--no cheap materials, plastic look, fake textures, obvious 3D render artifacts
--no oversaturated, HDR look, unrealistic colors, neon lighting
--no cluttered styling, too many decorations, messy room, dirty surfaces
--no generic stock photo feel, catalog look, showroom sterile
--no inconsistent style between rooms, mixed design languages
--no missing logo, no logo
```
**模式 R 追加：**
```text
--no different style, altered layout, changed materials, inconsistent with reference
```
**模式 I 追加：**
```text
--no inconsistent style between spaces, varying materials, different design language
```
**风格专用：**
```text
# Style A (Modern Minimal):
--no ornate details, busy patterns, warm wood tones, traditional elements, crown molding
# Style B (Light Luxury):
--no cheap materials, casual styling, industrial elements, bare bulbs
# Style C (Nordic):
--no dark colors, heavy furniture, ornate decoration, cold metals
# Style D (New Chinese):
--no western classical, modern industrial, bright colors, minimalist sterile
# Style E (Japanese):
--no bold colors, heavy decoration, western furniture, shiny surfaces
```
---
## 4) 设计公司 LOGO 设计模板
### 4.1 LOGO 变量配置
```yaml
LogoProject:
[LogoStyle]: [A / B]
# A = 现代建筑感（Geometric, architectural, minimal）
# B = 工艺匠心感（Refined serif, craft reference）
[LogoConcept]: "" # house abstract / floor plan / initial monogram / golden ratio / design tool
[Lockup]: Stacked / Horizontal
[BilingualLogo]: Yes / No
```
### 4.2 双语 LOGO Prompt
```text
=== INTERIOR DESIGN COMPANY LOGO — BILINGUAL (TEXTMODE A) ===
Design a professional INTERIOR DESIGN company logo with BOTH English and Chinese wordmarks.
Sophisticated, architectural, trustworthy, creative.
BRAND:
- English Name: [CompanyName_EN] (MUST render this exactly)
- Chinese Name: [CompanyName_CN] (MUST render this exactly)
- Category: Interior Design / Architecture / Home Design
- Personality: [品牌关键词]
ICON DESIGN:
CONCEPT: [LogoConcept 详细描述]
Requirements:
- Geometric, architectural feel
- 3-5 elements maximum
- Works in single color (print/emboss friendly)
- Readable at 16px
- No realistic house drawing, no complex illustration
STYLE:
[A] Modern Architectural: Clean geometric, abstract space/structure reference
[B] Craft Heritage: Refined typography, subtle craft/design tool reference
TEXT REQUIREMENTS (CRITICAL):
EN Render EXACTLY: "[CompanyName_EN]"
Letter-by-letter: [逐字母列出] ([X] letters)
CN Render EXACTLY: "[CompanyName_CN]"
Character-by-character: [逐字符列出] ([X] chars)
LAYOUT:
Stacked or Horizontal, balanced, wide letter-spacing.
COLOR:
Primary [C1], Secondary [C2]
Must work in: black, white, gold foil
--ar 1:1 --v 6.1 --style raw --q 2
--no misspelled text, wrong characters, realistic house, busy, 3D effects
```
---
## 5) 海报 12 张通用 Prompt
> **风格锚点策略**：Mode I 先跑 **KV02 客厅** 作为风格锚点 → 填 `AnchorURL`；其余全部 `--cref AnchorURL` 保持风格统一。
---
### KV01 整体设计概览｜DESIGN OVERVIEW
```text
=== INTERIOR KV 01: DESIGN OVERVIEW ===
[AR_POSTER], premium interior design presentation, 8K, editorial layout, Swiss grid.
CONCEPT:
Design overview / mood board style / project introduction
Show the essence of the entire design project.
LAYOUT OPTIONS:
A) Collage style: Key spaces as elegant thumbnails with connecting design elements
B) Hero + details: One large hero image + smaller detail shots
C) Mood board: Materials + colors + key furniture + space previews
CONTENT TO INCLUDE:
- Project name: "[ProjectName_EN] | [ProjectName_CN]"
- Style: [Style] aesthetic
- Key spaces preview (living, bedroom, kitchen glimpses)
- Material/color palette suggestion
- Design mood/atmosphere
STYLE:
Consistent with [Style] design language.
Premium magazine editorial quality.
Cohesive color palette based on [配色方案].
TYPOGRAPHY:
Project name large and elegant.
"[Tagline_EN]"
"[Tagline_CN]"
Highlights listed cleanly.
LOGO ([LogoPosition] mandatory):
[LogoStyle], color [LogoColor].
--ar [AR_POSTER] --v 6.1 --style raw --q 2
--no cluttered, inconsistent style, cheap look, stock photo feel
--no missing logo, misspelled
```

6. Stone / tile craftsmanship
7. Custom storage solution
8. Ceiling detail / lighting cove
9. Furniture craftsmanship
EACH DETAIL:
Macro or close-up photography.
Sharp focus on craftsmanship.
Beautiful natural or designed lighting.
Premium material quality evident.
LAYOUT:
Grid (3x3 or 2x3) or asymmetric elegant arrangement.
Consistent crop style (square or same AR).
Small labels optional.
COHESION:
All details from the same project.
Same photographic style and color grading.
Tells the story of quality and attention to detail.

## 6) cw 使用策略（室内设计版）
```yaml
Mode R:
KV01_Overview: 70
KV02_LivingRoom: 100
KV03_MasterBedroom: 85
KV04_SecondBedroom: 80
KV05_Kitchen: 85
KV06_DiningRoom: 80
KV07_MasterBath: 85
KV08_GuestBath: 80
KV09_Entryway: 80
KV10_Balcony: 75
KV11_Materials: 60
KV12_Details: 85
Mode I:
KV01_Overview: N/A (generate independently)
KV02_LivingRoom: N/A (this IS the anchor)
KV03_MasterBedroom: 80
KV04_SecondBedroom: 75
KV05_Kitchen: 80
KV06_DiningRoom: 80
KV07_MasterBath: 75
KV08_GuestBath: 70
KV09_Entryway: 75
KV10_Balcony: 70
KV11_Materials: 60
KV12_Details: 75
```

## 7) 室内设计光影指南
```yaml
InteriorLightingGuide:
核心原则:
自然光为主: "模拟真实居住环境的自然采光"
时间感: "暗示一天中的美好时刻（晨光/午后/黄昏）"
层次感: "自然光+人工光+氛围光的组合"
真实感: "避免过度渲染的HDR感"
各空间光线建议:
客厅:
日间: "大落地窗自然光，柔和漫射"
傍晚: "暖色人工光，无主灯氛围"
关键: "电视墙适当暗，沙发区明亮"
主卧:
首选: "晨光从窗户柔和射入"
备选: "傍晚暖光，床头灯亮起"
关键: "床品细节可见，整体温馨"
厨房:
首选: "明亮自然光+操作台任务光"
关键: "台面无暗角，橱柜层次清晰"
卫生间:
首选: "明亮均匀，镜前灯重点"
关键: "材质纹理可见，干净明亮"
玄关:
首选: "柔和引导光，与室内光线过渡"
关键: "储物柜细节可见"
阳台:
首选: "充足自然光，室内外过渡"
休闲: "黄昏金色光线"
色温指南:
日间场景: "5500-6000K 自然日光"
傍晚场景: "3500-4000K 暖白"
氛围场景: "2700-3000K 暖光"
避免:
- 过曝的窗户（保留细节）
- 死黑的角落（保持层次）
- 人工感过强的渲染光
- 不自然的彩色灯光
- HDR过度的效果
```
---
## 8) 质检清单（室内设计版）
```text
【LOGO】
□ 每张都有LOGO，位置正确，颜色正确
□ 公司名无错字（EN/CN）
【文字】
□ 空间名称正确显示
□ 无乱码、无切边、无重叠
□ 字体风格统一
【透视与比例】
□ 透视线正确，墙壁垂直
□ 家具比例真实（门高2m参照）
□ 空间尺度合理
□ 无变形、无弯曲
【材质真实感】
□ 木纹自然，不重复
□ 石材纹理真实
□ 布艺有质感
□ 金属光泽受控
□ 无明显3D渲染感
【风格一致性（最重要）】
□ 所有空间设计语言统一
□ 材质调色板统一
- 木色一致
- 石材/瓷砖风格一致
- 金属色调一致
□ 色彩体系统一
- 墙面色一致
- 点缀色协调
□ 设计元素统一
- 踢脚线风格
- 门套风格
- 灯具风格
□ 像同一个设计师做的同一套房
【空间功能合理性】
□ 动线合理
□ 家具布局合理
□ 储物解决方案实用
□ 采光充足
【光影质量】
□ 光线自然真实
□ 窗户不过曝
□ 暗角有细节
□ 明暗层次丰富
□ 色温协调
【摄影质量】
□ 构图专业（建筑摄影感）
□ 视角选择展示空间优势
□ 清晰锐利
□ 无畸变
```
---
## 9) 快速使用指南
```text
【完整项目出图流程】
1. 填写 STEP 1-3（项目+品牌信息）
2. 选择 Style A/B/C/D/E（统一风格）
3. 填写 STEP 5（整体配色方案）
4. 填写 STEP 9（空间规划）
5. 填写 STEP 10 各空间详细定义
6. 填写 STEP 11（风格统一锚点）—— 这是一致性的关键！
7. 填写 STEP 12-13（文案）
【生成顺序（重要）】
1. 先生成 KV02 客厅 → 作为风格锚点
2. 审核通过后，填入 AnchorURL
3. 按顺序生成其他空间（全部 --cref AnchorURL）
4. 最后生成 KV01概览、KV11材质板、KV12细节
【Mode R 简化流程】
1. 上传风格参考图 → RefImageURL
2. 填写项目信息 + 各空间需求
3. 直接按顺序生成
【核心图优先级】
若时间有限，优先生成：
1. KV02 客厅（必须/锚点）
2. KV03 主卧
3. KV05 厨房
4. KV07 主卫
5. KV12 细节集锦
```
---
## 10) 附录：风格速查表
| 风格 | 主要材质 | 色彩基调 | 关键元素 | 氛围 |
|------|----------|----------|----------|------|
| **A 现代简约** | 大板瓷砖、木饰面、金属 | 黑白灰+木色 | 无主灯、隐藏收纳、干净线条 | 克制理性 |
| **B 轻奢雅致** | 大理石、皮革、黄铜 | 奶油色+金色 | 精致五金、优雅灯具、层次感 | 精致高级 |
| **C 北欧温馨** | 原木、棉麻、藤编 | 白+原木+柔和彩 | 圆润家具、温暖纺织、绿植 | 舒适治愈 |
| **D 新中式** | 木石结合、丝绸、黄铜 | 米白+胡桃木+墨色 | 留白、意境、对称、书画 | 东方禅意 |
| **E 日式原木** | 浅色原木、纸、竹 | 木白色+米色 | 极简收纳、榻榻米、障子门 | 宁静素雅 |
---
## 11) 户型空间速查表
| 空间 | 核心卖点 | 重点展示 | 拍摄建议 |
|------|----------|----------|----------|
| **客厅** | 空间感/设计感/品质感 | 沙发区+电视墙+整体开阔 | 宽角度展示空间 |
| **主卧** | 舒适/私密/品质 | 床+床头墙+整体氛围 | 温馨氛围光 |
| **次卧** | 功能性/成长性 | 床+学习区/储物 | 展示多功能 |
| **厨房** | 功能/材质/整洁 | 橱柜+台面+电器 | 明亮整洁 |
| **餐厅** | 社交/家庭/设计 | 餐桌+吊灯 | 温暖邀请感 |
| **主卫** | 酒店感/spa感 | 洗手台+浴缸/淋浴 | 明亮高端 |
| **玄关** | 第一印象/收纳 | 鞋柜+整体设计 | 欢迎引导感 |
| **阳台** | 生活/休闲 | 功能区+与室内连接 | 自然光线 |
---
## 12) 常见问题解决
```text
【问题：各空间风格不统一】
解决：
1. 确保 STEP 11 风格锚点填写完整
2. KV02客厅必须作为锚点先生成
3. 其他空间全部 --cref AnchorURL
4. cw值适当提高（80-85）
【问题：透视变形】
解决：
1. 提示词加入 "architectural photography, straight verticals"
2. 负面词加入 "warped, distorted, bent walls, perspective error"
3. 选择更标准的视角（非极端广角）
【问题：渲染感过强】
解决：
1. 强调 "real interior photography, not 3D render"
2. 加入 "natural imperfections, lived-in feel"
3. 负面词加入 "CGI look, too perfect, sterile"
【问题：材质看起来假】
解决：
1. 具体描述材质细节（木纹方向、石材纹理）
2. 加入 "real materials, tactile quality"
3. 强调光线如何与材质互动
【问题：家具比例失调】
解决：
1. 提供尺寸参照（门高2m、沙发宽度等）
2. 负面词加入 "wrong scale, unrealistic proportions"
3. 参考真实家具品牌的比例
```
---
Part II End
```

---

### [历史长河里的爱情故事](https://aiart.pics/prompt/love-stories-from-the-long-river-of-history)

**作者**: [@大卫叔的AI旅程](https://x.com/aidavid125)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/aidavid125/status/2002222515792548210)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/love-stories-from-the-long-river-of-history-1.png" width="500" alt="历史长河里的爱情故事">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/love-stories-from-the-long-river-of-history-2.png" width="500" alt="历史长河里的爱情故事">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/love-stories-from-the-long-river-of-history-3.png" width="500" alt="历史长河里的爱情故事">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251220/love-stories-from-the-long-river-of-history-4.png" width="500" alt="历史长河里的爱情故事">

```
Love stories from a long history.
历史长河里的爱情故事.
Prompt is below ⬇
Prompt:
## Role：
**Midjourney 史诗浪漫视觉架构师 (Epic Romance Visual Architect)**
## Goal：
根据用户输入的国家名，将其核心浪漫文化转化为视觉符号。要求桥梁必须由该国最浪漫的物质**纯粹构成**（严禁出现石头、齿轮、机械材质）。左上角以**全大写英文**标注国家名。特别注意：**中国版背景不再使用长城，改为更具空灵神话感的天宫或星河。**
## Work Progress：
1. **文化符号映射**：
- **CHINA**：桥梁 = 鹊桥 (Magpie Bridge)，背景 = 缥缈天宫与星河 (Ethereal Heavenly Palace & Starry Void)，材质 = 灵动羽毛与墨雾。
- **UNITED KINGDOM / ITALY / FRANCE**：桥梁 = 玫瑰桥 (Rose Bridge)，背景 = 哥特建筑/标志性地标，材质 = 红色丝绒花瓣。
- **JAPAN**：桥梁 = 樱花桥 (Sakura Bridge)，背景 = 富士山 (Mount Fuji)，材质 = 粉色闪光花瓣。
- **其他国家**：提取代表性浪漫花卉或符号作为桥梁材质，地标作为虚幻背景。
2. **材质净化**：强制剔除石材、木材、齿轮、砖块等一切硬质建筑结构，确保桥梁是“流动”的。
3. **视觉布局**：设定 16:9 画幅，金箔英文国名置于左上角，主角半人半材质从桥面中心冲破而出。
4. **生成提示词**：输出纯英文的 Midjourney V6.0 专家级提示词。
## Standard Prompt Template:
> **Extreme wide-angle cinematic shot of an infinite, ethereal winding stream flowing through a dark, starlit celestial void, manifested ENTIRELY and SOLELY from a dense, living mass of [Bridge_Material].
> • The Form: This is a fluid, organic ribbon of romance; it has NO stone, NO gears, NO metal, NO masonry, and NO architectural structure. It is a celestial path manifested from [Symbol_Name].
> • Top-Left Corner Branding: The word "[COUNTRY_NAME_ENGLISH]" is elegantly inscribed in the top-left corner in bold, exquisite gold-leaf English serif typography.
> • The Love Story (Erupting): In the extreme foreground, a pair of legendary [Country_Name] lovers in [Historical_Attire] are dramatically emerging from the [Bridge_Material]. Their bodies are half-realistic flesh and half-ethereal [Material_Texture], reaching for a passionate, eternal embrace. Thousands of [Flying_Elements] are flying everywhere in 3D perspective.
> • Micro Details: Intense longing and glistening tears in their eyes, the intricate texture of their garments, and a soft, divine glow on their skin.
> • Background Grandeur: Deep in the misty stardust, the ghostly, shimmering silhouette of [Background_Landmark] rises from the cosmic clouds.
> • Atmosphere & Lighting: Divine "God rays" piercing through heavy charcoal clouds. Every edge has a sharp, blinding glint. Volumetric smoke and shimmering embers.
> • Technical Specs: Unreal Engine 5.3 render, 8k, Ray Tracing, extreme depth of field, IMAX quality. --ar 16:9 --stylize 1000 --v 6.0 --no stone bridge, gears, metal, machine, industrial, mechanical, wood, architecture, bricks, bridge base, masonry**
## Output Rule:
1. **国家名规范**：输出的提示词中 `Top-Left Corner Branding` 必须是**全大写英文**。
2. **背景逻辑**：输入“中国”时，背景设定为 `Ethereal Heavenly Palace`（空灵天宫），绝对不准出现长城。
3. **纯净材质**：严禁出现任何桥墩、栏杆或人造基座，桥梁必须看起来是由无数微小个体组成的群落。
---
## 示例演示 (Example Demo)
### 输入：中国
**Prompt**:
> Extreme wide-angle cinematic shot of an infinite, ethereal winding stream flowing through a dark, starlit celestial void, manifested ENTIRELY and SOLELY from a dense, living mass of **millions of fluttering black-and-white magpies**. • The Form: This is a living, organic ribbon of birds; it has NO stone, NO gears, NO metal, and NO architectural parts. • Top-Left Corner Branding: The word "**CHINA**" is elegantly inscribed in the top-left corner in bold, exquisite gold-leaf English serif typography. • The Love Story (Erupting): In the extreme foreground, a pair of legendary Chinese lovers in **flowing silk Hanfu** are dramatically emerging from the swirling magpies. Their bodies are half-realistic flesh and **half-indigo feathers**, reaching for a passionate embrace. Thousands of **glowing feathers and stardust** are flying everywhere. • Micro Details: Tears of longing, intricate silk textures, and a soft pearlescent glow on skin. • Background Grandeur: Deep in the misty stardust, the **ghostly, shimmering silhouette of an ethereal Heavenly Palace** rises from the cosmic clouds of the Milky Way. • Atmosphere & Lighting: Divine "God rays" piercing through indigo clouds. --ar 16:9 --stylize 1000 --v 6.0 --no stone bridge, gears, metal, machine, industrial, mechanical, wood, architecture, bricks, bridge base, masonry, Great Wall
### 输入：英国
**Prompt**:
> Extreme wide-angle cinematic shot of an infinite, ethereal winding stream flowing through a dark, starlit celestial void, manifested ENTIRELY and SOLELY from a dense, living mass of **billions of blooming deep red roses**. • The Form: This is a fluid, organic ribbon of roses; it has NO stone, NO architecture. • Top-Left Corner Branding: The word "**UNITED KINGDOM**" is inscribed in the top-left corner in bold, gold-leaf serif typography. • The Love Story (Erupting): A pair of iconic British lovers in **Victorian velvet and lace** are dramatically emerging from the red rose bridge. Their bodies are half-realistic flesh and **half-crimson petals**. Thousands of **shattering rose petals** are flying everywhere. • Background Grandeur: Deep in the background, the **ghostly silhouette of a Gothic cathedral** rises from the cosmic clouds. --ar 16:9 --stylize 1000 --v 6.0 --no stone bridge, gears, metal, machine, industrial, mechanical, wood, architecture, bricks, bridge base, masonry
### 输入：日本
**Prompt**:
> Extreme wide-angle cinematic shot of an infinite, ethereal winding stream flowing through a dark, starlit celestial void, manifested ENTIRELY and SOLELY from a dense, **swirling vortex of pink Sakura petals**. • The Form: This is a soft, organic ribbon of cherry blossoms; it has NO stone, NO architecture. • Top-Left Corner Branding: The word "**JAPAN**" is inscribed in the top-left corner in bold, gold-leaf serif typography. • The Love Story (Erupting): A pair of Japanese lovers in **exquisite patterned Kimonos** are emerging from the Sakura vortex. Their bodies are half-realistic flesh and **half-shimmering petals**. Thousands of **fluttering Sakura petals** are flying everywhere. • Background Grandeur: Deep in the background, the **ethereal silhouette of Mount Fuji** rises. --ar 16:9 --stylize 1000 --v 6.0 --no stone bridge, gears, metal, machine, industrial, mechanical, wood, architecture, bricks, bridge base, masonry
---------------------------------
Input the Country Name.
Welcome to optimize and improve.

## Role:
**Midjourney Epic Romance Visual Architect**
## Goal:
Based on the user-inputted country name, transform its core romantic culture into visual symbols. The central bridge must be **purely composed** of the country's most romantic substance (strictly prohibiting stone, gears, or mechanical materials). The top-left corner must feature the country name in **ALL-CAPS English**. Special Instruction: **For China, the background must no longer use the Great Wall; it should be replaced with an ethereal, mythical Heavenly Palace or a Starry Void.**
## Work Progress:
1. **Cultural Symbol Mapping**:
* **CHINA**: Bridge = Magpie Bridge (Que Qiao), Background = Ethereal Heavenly Palace & Starry Void, Material = Ethereal feathers and ink-mist.
* **UNITED KINGDOM / ITALY / FRANCE**: Bridge = Rose Bridge, Background = Gothic architecture/Iconic landmarks, Material = Red velvet petals.
* **JAPAN**: Bridge = Sakura Bridge, Background = Mount Fuji, Material = Shimmering pink petals.
* **OTHER COUNTRIES**: Extract representative romantic flowers or symbols as the bridge material and use dreamlike landmarks as the background.

> • Technical Specs: Unreal Engine 5.3 render, 8k, Ray Tracing, extreme depth of field, IMAX quality. --ar 16:9 --stylize 1000 --v 6.0 --no stone bridge, gears, metal, machine, industrial, mechanical, wood, architecture, bricks, bridge base, masonry**

### [历史画卷文化分析](https://aiart.pics/prompt/historical-scroll-painting-cultural-analysis)

**作者**: [@大卫叔的AI旅程](https://x.com/aidavid125)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/aidavid125/thread/2001086582204649734)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251218/historical-scroll-painting-cultural-analysis-1.jpg" width="500" alt="历史画卷文化分析">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251218/historical-scroll-painting-cultural-analysis-2.jpg" width="500" alt="历史画卷文化分析">

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251218/historical-scroll-painting-cultural-analysis-3.jpg" width="500" alt="历史画卷文化分析">

```
历史画卷里的文化：
敦煌飞天舞，四川民间变脸艺术，少林功夫。
提示词评论区见 https://t.co/f63Q4DU1nm
提示词：
Hyper-realistic 3D masterpiece, set against a magnificent, endless traditional ink-wash historical scroll painting unfurling across the background.The scene visualizes the cultural soul and intangible heritage of [在此处填入地点或主题], featuring [在此处填入具体形象，如：a Flying Apsara playing the Pipa / a Peking Opera warrior] leaping vividly from the scroll.• Composition: The character breaks the fourth wall, transitioning from the flat paper into the 3D space. Dynamic pose capturing a moment of peak action.• Visual Effect: 2D black ink brushstrokes on the paper surface morph seamlessly into high-fidelity 3D realistic skin, flowing silk fabrics, and exquisite embroidery.• Details: Faded ancient parchment texture, floating historical calligraphy characters, red seal stamps, [可选细节：falling flower petals / glowing musical notes / swirling smoke].• Lighting: Dramatic stage lighting or ethereal divine glow illuminating the character, contrasting with the monochrome ink background. Subsurface scattering on skin.• Specs: 8K resolution, high detail, Unreal Engine 5 render, cinematic composition.--ar 16:9 --stylize 350 --no buildings, rigid structures, modern clothing, cartoons, low resolution
----------------------------
变脸艺术：
[具体形象] ：a Sichuan Opera performer changing masks, breathing fire

```json
The Ultimate Master Prompt (Copy & Use)
Here's the complete Nano Banana Pro JSON template that combines all 9 tips.
Copy this, customize it, and generate perfect images every time:
THE MASTER PROMPT TEMPLATE:
{
"generation_mode": "thinking|standard",
"output_specifications": {
"resolution": "1K|2K|4K",
"aspect_ratio": "16:9|1:1|9:16|custom",
"quality_priority": "speed|balanced|quality"
},
"scene_description": {
"primary_subject": "[main focus of image]",
"environment": "[setting and background]",
"atmosphere": "[mood and feeling]",
"style": "[visual aesthetic]",
"time_of_day": "[if relevant]"
},
"camera_controls": {
"angle": "[camera perspective]",
"focal_length": "[lens type - wide/standard/telephoto]",
"depth_of_field": "[shallow/deep, what\'s in focus]",
"composition": "[rule of thirds/centered/golden ratio/etc]"
},
"lighting_setup": {
"primary_light": {
"type": "[natural/studio/dramatic/soft]",
"direction": "[where light comes from]",
"intensity": "[bright/moderate/moody]"
},
"shadows": "[deep/subtle/minimal]",
"color_temperature": "[warm/cool/neutral]",
"special_effects": "[rim light/backlighting/etc if needed]"
},
"color_grading": {
"overall_tone": "[vibrant/muted/monochrome/etc]",
"color_palette": ["primary color", "secondary color", "accent color"],
"mood": "[emotional impact of colors]"
},
"text_elements": [
{
"text_content": "[exact text to render]",
"position": "[location in image]",
"font_style": "[typography description]",
"size": "[relative size]",
"color": "[text color]",
"effects": "[glow/shadow/3D/etc]",
"language": "[if not English]"
}
],
"reference_images": [
{
"image_id": 1,
"purpose": "style reference|composition reference|color reference|character reference",
"extract_elements": ["specific elements to copy"],
"apply_to": "[where to use these elements]",
"transfer_intensity": "[0-100%]"
}
],
"characters": [
{
"character_id": 1,
"detailed_description": "[ethnicity, age, gender, facial features, hair, expression]",
"clothing": "[detailed outfit description]",
"pose": "[body position and gesture]",
"position_in_scene": "[spatial placement]",
"consistency_reference": "[image_id if maintaining across multiple generations]"
}
],
"grounding": {
"enabled": true|false,
"search_queries": ["facts to verify"],
"data_requirements": ["specific information needed"],
"accuracy_priority": "high|medium"
},
"style_constraints": {
"artistic_style": "[photorealistic/illustration/3D render/watercolor/etc]",
"inspiration": "[specific artists or movements if relevant]",
"must_avoid": ["elements to exclude"]
},
"technical_requirements": {
"intended_use": "[social media/print/web/presentation]",
"safe_zones": "[areas to keep clear for text/cropping]",
"brand_guidelines": ["colors/fonts/logos to include"]
},
"consistency_requirements": {
"maintain_across_series": true|false,
"locked_elements": ["elements that must stay identical"],
"variable_elements": ["what can change between generations"]
}
}
Use this master template for ANY image generation task. Just fill in your specific details.
Perfect images. Every time. No more wasted generations.
```

Tip 2: Use Text Rendering Parameters
Nano Banana Pro's secret weapon? Perfect text rendering in images.

Template Prompt:

"scene": "[your image description]",
"text_elements": [
{

"font_style": "[typography style]",

}
]
}

### [简约布景纳米香蕉专业摄影](https://aiart.pics/prompt/minimalist-beige-studio-photo-nano-banana-pro)

**作者**: [@Pawan | AI Tech Girl](https://x.com/AITechGirl)

**来源**: [X](https://x.com/AITechGirl/status/1997752643138298206)

<img src="https://img1.aiart.pics/images/prompts/20251213/minimalist-beige-studio-photo-nano-banana-pro-1.jpg" width="500" alt="简约布景纳米香蕉专业摄影">

```
Try this 👇Studio Photo Nano Banana Pro 🍌 Prompt
Follow ➡️ @AITechGirl For More, I ♥ your comments
Editorial 3x3 photo grid in a clean soft beige studio.
Character (matches reference 100%) wearing lightweight dark navy shirt, ivory trousers, barefoot for raw simplicity.
Lighting: large diffused key light directly front-right, silver reflector left, subtle rim from top.
Shots to include: 1. extreme close-up of lips + cheekbone with blurred hand partially covering (85mm, f/1.8, razor-thin DOF);
2. tight crop on eyes looking into lens with reflection of light strip visible (85mm, f/2.0);
3. black & white close portrait resting chin on fist, face filling frame (50mm, f/2.2);
4. over-shoulder shot, blurred foreground fabric curtain framing half face (85mm, f/2.0);
5. very close frontal with hands overlapping face, light streak across eyes (50mm, f/2.5);
6. tight angled portrait showing hair falling into eyes, soft-focus background (85mm, f/2.2);
7. crop of hands touching jawline, eyes cropped out (50mm, f/3.2, detail-focused);
8. half-body seated sideways on low cube, head turned sharply away, blurred foreground (35mm, f/ 4.5);
9. intense close-up of profile with single tear-like water droplet, cinematic light slice across (85mm, f/ 1.9).
Angles: mostly tight headshots with slight high/lo
